# PRFMR — Mobile Replication Guide

Complete specification for replicating PRFMR in a new Replit project.  
Target: a React Native / Expo mobile app (or a second PWA) that is **functionally identical** to the existing web app.

## 1. App Overview & Vision

PRFMR is a **mobile-first nutrition and training tracker** built for combat athletes (MMA, boxing, wrestling, BJJ) and other high-performance athletes. It sits in the gap between generic calorie counters (MyFitnessPal) and coach-led software — giving a solo athlete the data-driven tools a sports nutritionist would use.

**Core user jobs-to-be-done:**
- Know exactly how many calories and macros to eat today (adjusted for training)
- Log food fast without manual lookup (barcode, quick-add, natural language)
- Understand micronutrient quality, not just macros
- Plan and execute a fight-camp weight cut with daily guidance
- Track training load and avoid overtraining

**Design philosophy:**
- Conservative framing — never over-promise
- Transparent calculations — show the maths
- Dark theme throughout
- Mobile-first layout (max-width ~430px cards, bottom-nav style)
- Space Grotesk for headings, Inter for body text

---

## 2. Technology Stack

### Frontend
| Concern | Choice |
|---|---|
| Framework | React 18 + TypeScript |
| Build tool | Vite |
| Routing | Wouter |
| Server state | TanStack React Query v5 |
| Styling | Tailwind CSS + shadcn/ui (Radix UI) |
| Animation | Framer Motion |
| Charts | Recharts |
| Forms | react-hook-form + zodResolver |
| Icons | lucide-react + react-icons/si |
| Barcode scanner | html5-qrcode |

### Backend
| Concern | Choice |
|---|---|
| Runtime | Node.js + Express (TypeScript, ESM) |
| ORM | Drizzle ORM |
| Database | PostgreSQL |
| Sessions | connect-pg-simple + express-session |
| Auth | Passport.js (local + Google OAuth 2.0) |
| Password hashing | Argon2 |
| Email | Resend |
| File storage | Replit Object Storage |
| Push | web-push (VAPID) |

### Shared
- `shared/schema.ts` — single source of truth for all Drizzle table definitions, Zod insert schemas, and TypeScript types
- `shared/routes.ts` — typed route constants (API path + method, shared between client and server)
- `shared/weight-cut.ts` — pure weight-cut calculation engine (no DB, no Express)
- `shared/utils.ts` — `getMicronutrientValue()` and other helpers

## 3. Database Schema (all tables)

All tables are defined with Drizzle ORM in `shared/schema.ts`.  
Column types: `serial`, `integer`, `real`, `text`, `boolean`, `timestamp`, `jsonb`.

### 3.1 `users_auth` — Authentication records
```
id            serial PK
username      text UNIQUE NOT NULL
email         text UNIQUE
passwordHash  text
googleId      text UNIQUE
displayName   text
emailVerified boolean default false
isAdmin       boolean default false
createdAt     timestamp
```

### 3.2 `users` — Profile + calculated targets
```
id                  serial PK (same id as users_auth)
username            text FK
gender              text  ('male'|'female')
age                 integer
height              integer  (cm)
weight              real     (kg)
activityLevel       text     ('sedentary'|'light'|'moderate'|'active'|'very_active')

experienceLevel     text     ('beginner'|'intermediate'|'advanced')
bodyFatPct          real
targetCalories      integer
targetProtein       integer
targetCarbs         integer
targetFat           integer
profilePhotoUrl     text
fightCampActive     boolean  default false
fightDate           text     (YYYY-MM-DD)
weighInTiming       text     ('same_day'|'day_before')
onboardingComplete  boolean  default false
-- Onboarding survey fields (all text unless noted):
surveyCutExperience
surveyCutOutcome
surveyCalorieKnowledge
```

## 4. Backend Architecture

```
server/
  index.ts              Express app entry — session, passport, route registration, seeding
  auth.ts               Passport.js configuration (local + Google OAuth strategies, requireAuth middleware)
  auth-routes.ts        Mounted at /api/auth — all authentication endpoints
  invite-routes.ts      Mounted at /api/invites — invite request + validation
  feedback-routes.ts    Absolute paths /api/feedback/* — feedback submission + attachments
  routes.ts             All remaining API handlers (~4279 lines)
  storage.ts            IStorage interface + storage singleton export
  database-storage.ts   DrizzleStorage — implements IStorage against PostgreSQL
  db.ts                 Drizzle ORM + PostgreSQL pool setup
  seed-catalogs.ts      On-startup catalog seeder (exercises, activities, supplements, ingredients)
  vite.ts               Vite dev-server integration (development only)
  static.ts             Static file serving (production only)
  lib/
    amqs.ts             AMQS scoring engine
    micros.ts           Micronutrient extraction + COMPOSITE_FOODS map
    energy.ts           Calorie burn helpers — MET formula, RPE adjustment, lifting estimator
    readiness.ts        Session Readiness Score composite
    fuel-availability.ts  Fuel / glycogen pre-session status
    training-load.ts    ACWR, load classification, lifting calorie estimates
    email.ts            Resend email helper (verification, welcome, password reset, invites)
    push-notifications.ts  VAPID web-push helpers
    verification-tokens.ts  Email verification token generation/validation
    password-reset-tokens.ts  Password reset token generation/validation
    version.ts          App version + environment helpers
    beta-cap.ts         Active user count + beta limit helpers
    offMatch.ts         Open Food Facts ingredient auto-matching logic
    searchRanking.ts    Food search ranking/sorting logic
    provisional-readiness.ts  Provisional check-in status logic
    weight-cut.ts       (mirrors shared/weight-cut.ts — server-side import alias)
  replit_integrations/
    object_storage/
      routes.ts         Object storage upload/download routes
      objectStorage.ts  ObjectStorageService class
      objectAcl.ts      ACL helpers for public/private paths

shared/
  schema.ts             All Drizzle tables, Zod insert schemas, TypeScript types
  routes.ts             Typed API route constants
  weight-cut.ts         Pure weight-cut calculation functions
  utils.ts              getMicronutrientValue() and helpers
  username-validation.ts  validateUsername(), normalizeUsername(), RESERVED_USERNAMES

data/
  ingredients.json      307 ingredients with full macro + micro data (see §26)
```

### Route mounting order (server/routes.ts `registerRoutes()`)
```
app.use("/api/auth",    authRoutes)          → auth-routes.ts endpoints
app.use("/api/invites", inviteRoutes)         → invite-routes.ts endpoints
app.use(feedbackRoutes)                       → /api/feedback/* direct paths
registerObjectStorageRoutes(app)              → /api/objects/*
GET /auth/google                             → Google OAuth redirect
GET /auth/google/callback                    → Google OAuth callback
... all remaining /api/* routes from routes.ts
```

### Global middleware
- `express.json()` — parses JSON bodies, stores rawBody on request
- `express.urlencoded({ extended: false })` — URL-encoded bodies
- `setupAuth(app)` — installs session middleware, Passport, local + Google strategies
- All `/api` routes have `Cache-Control: no-store` headers set globally

### Authentication guard (`getAuthenticatedUser`)
Every protected route in `routes.ts` calls this helper first:
```typescript
async function getAuthenticatedUser(req, res): Promise<{ authUser, profileUser } | null>
// Returns null and sends 401/404 if not authenticated or profile not found
// authUser → from usersAuth table (session), profileUser → from users table
```

### Storage interface pattern
All database operations flow through `IStorage` (in `server/storage.ts`).  
Routes call `storage.someMethod(args)` — never raw Drizzle in routes.  
`DrizzleStorage` in `server/database-storage.ts` implements the interface against PostgreSQL.

### `calculateTargets()` — exported from routes.ts
```typescript
calculateTargets({ gender, weight, height, age, activityLevel, goal }): {
  bmr: number,
  tdee: number,
  targetCalories: number,
  targetProtein: number,
  targetFat: number,
  targetCarbs: number,
  trainingCalorieCreditPct: number,
  goal: string,
}
```
Also exported: `TRAINING_CALORIE_CREDIT_PCT = { fat_loss: 0.5, maintenance: 0.75, weight_gain: 1.0, fight_camp: 0.5 }`

---

## 5. Calculation Engine

All core maths lives in `server/routes.ts` `calculateTargets()` and `shared/weight-cut.ts`.

### 5.1 BMR — Mifflin-St Jeor
```
BMR = (10 × weight_kg) + (6.25 × height_cm) − (5 × age)
      + 5   (male)
      − 161 (female)
```

### 5.2 TDEE
```
Multipliers:
  sedentary   × 1.2
  light       × 1.375
  moderate    × 1.55
  active      × 1.725
  very_active × 1.9

TDEE = BMR × multiplier
```

### 5.3 Goal-based calorie targets
| Goal | Calories | Protein | Fat |
|---|---|---|---|
| fat_loss | TDEE − 500 | 2.2 g/kg | 0.7 g/kg |
| maintenance | TDEE | 1.8 g/kg | 0.8 g/kg |
| weight_gain | TDEE + 300 | 1.8 g/kg | 0.9 g/kg |

### 5.4 Dynamic carbs
```
Carbs = (targetCalories − (protein × 4) − (fat × 9)) / 4
```
Carbs are always the residual macro — protein and fat are fixed first.

### 5.5 Training calorie credits
When the user logs a training session, extra calories are added back:
```
Credit pct:
  fat_loss    → 50%
  maintenance → 75%
  weight_gain → 100%

Adjusted target calories = base target + (sessionKcal × creditPct)
```

### 5.6 Fight Camp target override
Priority order (highest wins):
1. **Fight Camp Active** — macro model driven by `weighInTiming` and weeks to fight
2. **Profile Goal** (fat_loss / maintenance / weight_gain)
3. **Maintenance fallback**

Fight camp models:
- `same_day` cut: more aggressive deficit, lower carbs
- `day_before` cut: moderate deficit, carb management before rehydration window

---

## 6. AMQS — Athlete Micronutrient Quality Score

Defined in `server/lib/amqs.ts`. Returns a score 0–100 and tier label.

### 6.1 Tracked nutrients (17 total)

The micro keys used throughout the codebase (in `ingredients.json`, `MICRO_KEYS` array in `micros.ts`, and `supplement_catalog.microsPerUnit`) use the suffix format below. **Use these exact key names** when building the data model.

| DB/JSON key | Display name | L1 Baseline Target | L2 Athlete Target |
|---|---|---|---|
| `vitamin_c_mg` | Vitamin C | 90 mg | 200 mg |
| `vitamin_d_ug` | Vitamin D | 20 mcg | 50 mcg |
| `vitamin_b12_ug` | Vitamin B12 | 2.4 mcg | 4 mcg |
| `vitamin_b6_mg` | Vitamin B6 | 1.7 mg | 3 mg |
| `folate_ug` | Folate | 400 mcg | 600 mcg |
| `vitamin_a_ug` | Vitamin A | 900 mcg | 1200 mcg |
| `vitamin_b2_mg` | Vitamin B2 (Riboflavin) | 1.3 mg | 2 mg |
| `vitamin_b1_mg` | Vitamin B1 (Thiamine) | 1.2 mg | 2 mg |
| `vitamin_b3_mg` | Vitamin B3 (Niacin) | 16 mg | 25 mg |
| `iron_mg` | Iron | 8 mg (M) / 18 mg (F) | 12 mg (M) / 25 mg (F) |
| `calcium_mg` | Calcium | 1000 mg | 1300 mg |
| `magnesium_mg` | Magnesium | 420 mg (M) / 320 mg (F) | 500 mg |
| `zinc_mg` | Zinc | 11 mg (M) / 8 mg (F) | 14 mg (M) / 11 mg (F) |
| `potassium_mg` | Potassium | 3500 mg | 4700 mg |
| `iodine_ug` | Iodine | 150 mcg | 200 mcg |
| `omega3_g` | Omega-3 | 1.1 g | 3 g |
| `selenium_ug` | Selenium | 55 mcg | 70 mcg |

`ingredients.json` stores each micro as `{key}_per_100g` (e.g. `iron_mg_per_100g`). All values are per 100 g of the ingredient (cooked basis where a `cookFactor` applies).

### 6.2 Two-layer scoring model

**L1 — Baseline Adequacy (50% of score)**  
Linear 0→1 as intake moves from 0 → L1 target.

**L2 — Athlete Optimization (50% of score)**  
Linear 0→1 as intake moves from L1 target → L2 target.

Per nutrient: `nutrientScore = (L1score × 0.5) + (L2score × 0.5)`  
Total: `rawScore = average(nutrientScore × weight) × 100`

Nutrient weights vary (critical nutrients get higher weight):
- Critical (iron, calcium, vitD, magnesium, zinc): weight 1.5
- Important (omega3, vitB12, potassium, fibre, vitC): weight 1.2
- Standard: weight 1.0

### 6.3 Elite gate
A score can only reach the "Elite" tier if **all critical nutrients** (iron, calcium, vitD, magnesium, zinc) are at ≥70% of their L1 target.

### 6.4 Tier thresholds
| Score | Tier |
|---|---|
| ≥ 95 | Elite |
| ≥ 85 | Optimal |
| ≥ 70 | Good |
| ≥ 50 | Fair |
| < 50 | Basic |

> **Note on Elite cap:** Even with a score ≥ 95, the tier is downgraded to **Optimal** if any of the six *critical nutrients* (Vitamin D, Magnesium, Zinc, Iron, Omega-3, Calcium) falls below 70% of its Layer-1 target.

### 6.5 Confidence rating
Based on % of food entries that have micronutrient data:
- 0–30%: Low
- 31–60%: Medium
- 61–100%: High

### 6.6 Supplement micros → AMQS connection (full frontend spec)

#### How supplements feed the score
Supplement intakes for the day are aggregated server-side and added to food micronutrient totals before AMQS scoring. Formula: `microsPerUnit × doseAmount` from `supplement_catalog.microsPerUnit`. Only intakes marked `taken === true` on that date count. Only catalog-linked supplements (non-null `catalogId`) contribute — custom supplements with no catalog link contribute zero.

The merged total is served by `GET /api/me/amqs/micros/:date` and is what the server uses when computing `GET /api/me/amqs/score/:date`.

#### What the AMQS score API returns (supplement-relevant fields)
```typescript
// GET /api/me/amqs/score/:date response
{
  score: number
  tier: string
  confidence: "Low" | "Medium" | "High"
  totals: Record<string, number>       // combined food + supplement intake per nutrient
  breakdown: {
    food:        Record<string, number> // food-only intake per nutrient
    supplements: Record<string, number> // supplement-only intake per nutrient
  }
  coverageStats: {
    totalTakenSupplements?: number      // # of supplements marked taken today
  }
  topGaps: { microKey, label, pctOfTarget, suggestion? }[]
  allMet: boolean
  // ... layer2 fields
}
```

#### Frontend signals driven by supplement data

**1. Empty state gate (AMQSCard)**
The card shows data (not the empty/provisional state) when either:
- `daily.confidence !== "Low"` AND `daily.score > 0` (`hasFoodToday`), **OR**
- `daily.coverageStats?.totalTakenSupplements > 0` (`hasSupplementsToday`)

This means: **if a user has taken supplements but logged no food**, the AMQS card still exits the empty state and shows a real score.

**2. "What moved it" subtitle (AMQSCard)**
This one-line summary on the main card is computed from `daily.breakdown`:
```
combined = { ...breakdown.food } merged with { ...breakdown.supplements }
topEntry = highest-value nutrient across the combined map
```
Output format: `"+{value}% {NutrientLabel} · {gap.label} at {pct}%"`

A supplement micro (e.g. Vitamin D from a Vitamin D3 supplement) will appear as the top contributor if it is the largest nutrient value in the combined breakdown — the card does not distinguish food vs supplement in this text.

**3. "AMQS tracked" badge on supplement shelf**
Any supplement with a non-null `catalogId` shows:
- `<Badge variant="default" className="text-[10px]">AMQS tracked</Badge>`
- Sub-line: `<p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground/60 mt-0.5">Contributing to your AMQS score</p>`

Important nuance: supplements with a `catalogId` but an empty `microsPerUnit: {}` (e.g. Creatine, Vitamin K2) still show the "AMQS tracked" badge, but they contribute zero micros to the score. The badge means "linked to catalog", not necessarily "moves the score".

**4. Cache invalidation on supplement mutations**
Any add, edit, or delete of a supplement immediately invalidates:
```
["/api/me/amqs/score"]        (exact: false — all date variants)
["/api/me/amqs/score-range"]  (exact: false — all range variants)
```
This ensures the AMQS card refreshes as soon as a supplement is saved or removed.

**5. Baseline completion — three related UI elements**

When all Layer-1 targets are met (`daily.allMet === true`), three separate UI elements respond. These are independent — replicate all three.

**5a. One-time toast**

Triggered by a `useEffect` watching `[daily?.allMet, date]`:

```typescript
useEffect(() => {
  if (!daily || !daily.allMet) return;
  const key = `amqs-l1-complete-${date}`;           // date = "YYYY-MM-DD"
  if (localStorage.getItem(key)) return;             // already fired today — skip
  localStorage.setItem(key, "1");                    // mark as fired
  toast({
    title: "Baseline adequacy covered",
    description: "All key micronutrient targets met today. Now optimise for athlete targets.",
    duration: 5000,
  });
}, [daily?.allMet, date]);
```

Key rules:
- The localStorage key is `amqs-l1-complete-{date}` (e.g. `amqs-l1-complete-2026-06-21`). A new key is created per calendar day so the toast re-fires on a new day if the user hits the target again.
- The toast fires at most once per day, even if the component re-renders or the user navigates away and back.
- The `date` prop comes from the dashboard's `selectedDate` state — it is the date currently in view, not necessarily today.
- The toast uses the standard `useToast` hook (shadcn `Toaster`). No custom variant — it renders as a default toast.

**5b. Inline card callout (replaces top-gaps list)**

When `daily.allMet === true`, the "Top gaps" section at the bottom of the main AMQS card is **replaced** by this green callout:

```
data-testid="amqs-all-met"
className="pt-3"

Inner div: "flex items-center gap-2 p-3 rounded-lg bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20"
  <ShieldCheck className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-500 shrink-0" />
  <p className="text-xs text-emerald-600 dark:text-emerald-400 font-medium leading-tight">
    Baseline adequacy covered. Tap to see athlete optimisation targets.
  </p>
```

This callout is shown instead of the `topGaps` bars. The card remains tappable (opens the detail dialog) so the user can view Layer-2 athlete targets.

**5c. Detail dialog callout (score ≥ 85, not strictly tied to allMet)**

Inside the AMQS detail dialog, when `daily.score >= 85`, a separate green callout appears above the gaps lists:

```
data-testid="callout-layer1-strong"
className="flex items-start gap-2 p-3 rounded-lg bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20"

  <ShieldCheck className="h-4 w-4 text-emerald-500 shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
  <p className="text-xs text-emerald-600 dark:text-emerald-400 leading-relaxed">
    Baseline micronutrient needs covered. If you're training hard, consider optimising
    toward athlete targets.
  </p>
```

Note: this triggers at `score >= 85`, not at `allMet`. A user can have `allMet === true` with a score below 85 (or vice versa) — they are independent conditions. Both can be visible simultaneously inside the dialog.

**6. AMQS detail dialog footer disclaimer**
The detail dialog (opened by tapping the AMQS card) always shows at the bottom:
```
"Based on logged foods and supplements. Estimates only; not medical advice."
```

---

## 7. Session Readiness Score

> ⚠️ **ALL calculations happen on the server.** The frontend (`SessionReadiness.tsx`) is pure display — it renders what the API returns verbatim. Do NOT re-implement scoring logic in the mobile client.

### 7.1 Endpoint

```
GET /api/me/readiness/:date        (date = YYYY-MM-DD)
```

Returns a single JSON object. Render it directly.

### 7.2 How the score is built (server-side)

The server gathers data for **today** (date param) and **yesterday** (date - 1), then computes four component scores and sums them.

#### Component 1 — Sleep (max 30 pts)
Source: `GET /api/me/sleep/:date` (today's sleep log — hours + quality rating 1–5)

| Hours slept | Base score |
|---|---|
| ≥ 8.0 h | 30 |
| ≥ 7.0 h | 26 |
| ≥ 6.0 h | 20 |
| ≥ 5.0 h | 14 |
| < 5.0 h | 8 |

Quality adjustment (applied to base): quality ≥ 4 → +2; quality ≤ 2 → −2; otherwise 0.
Score is clamped to [0, 30]. If no sleep log exists, score = 0 and `missingData` includes `"sleep"`.

#### Component 2 — Energy Availability (max 30 pts)
Source: yesterday's food log calories + exercise kcal from yesterday's sessions.

```
FFM (kg)  = bodyweightKg × (1 − bodyFatPct)   [bodyFatPct defaults 0.15 if not set]
EA (raw)  = (caloriesYesterday − exerciseKcalYesterday) / FFM
```

The server computes a **3-day smoothed EA** (rolling average of the last 3 days with food data). Smoothed EA is used for scoring when available; raw EA is shown in the UI detail.

| EA for scoring (smoothed or raw) | Score |
|---|---|
| ≥ 40 kcal/kg FFM | 30 |
| ≥ 35 | 25 |
| ≥ 30 | 18 |
| ≥ 25 | 10 |
| < 25 | 5 |

If bodyweight is unavailable, score = 15 (neutral fallback).

#### Component 3 — Carb Sufficiency (max 25 pts)
Source: yesterday's carb intake (g) + today's training load classification.

Carb target is determined by **today's** training demand:

| Today's classification | Target g/kg |
|---|---|
| light | 3 |
| moderate | 5 |
| hard | 6 |
| very_hard | 7 |

```
carbsPerKg = carbsYesterdayG / bodyweightKg
pct        = carbsYesterdayG / (target_g_per_kg × bodyweightKg)
score      = clamp(round(pct × 25), 0, 25)   ← proportional, not stepped
```

#### Component 4 — AMQS (max 15 pts)
Source: yesterday's AMQS score (from `computeAMQSScore` — same logic as §6).

| AMQS score | Points |
|---|---|
| ≥ 85 | 15 |
| ≥ 75 | 12 |
| ≥ 60 | 9 |
| < 60 | 5 |

#### Total and label

```
total = sleepScore + energyScore + carbScore + amqsScore   (max 100)
```

| Total | Label |
|---|---|
| ≥ 85 | High |
| ≥ 70 | Moderate |
| ≥ 55 | Low |
| < 55 | Poor |
| any missing data | Provisional |

Missing data (`missingData[]`) is triggered only by **sleep not logged**. Missing yesterday's food or training does NOT currently mark readiness as provisional (the server treats absent training as rest and absent food as 0 kcal).

### 7.3 Provisional mode

When `provisional: true` (sleep not logged) AND the user has completed a Morning Check-In (`ProvisionalCheckin`), the server computes `provisionalReadiness` via `calculateProvisionalReadiness()` in `server/lib/provisional-readiness.ts`.

Provisional scoring is purely self-report based:

| Answer | Field | Score |
|---|---|---|
| Fresh / Okay / Tired | `feelScore` | 40 / 28 / 16 |
| Yes / Somewhat / No (fueled) | `fuelScore` | 40 / 25 / 10 |
| Light / Moderate / Hard (intensity) | `intensityScore` | 20 / 15 / 10 |

Training penalty (from yesterday's sessions, resolved server-side): hard = −8, moderate = −4, light = −2, none = 0.

```
provisionalScore = feelScore + fuelScore + intensityScore + trainingPenalty
```

| Score | Label |
|---|---|
| ≥ 80 | Good |
| ≥ 65 | Moderate |
| ≥ 50 | Caution |
| < 50 | Low |

### 7.4 Load stacking detection (server-side)

The server runs `computeLoadWarnings()` comparing today's load against the previous 2 days. Results arrive as booleans in the response:

| Field | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `backToBackHardDays` | Hard session yesterday and today |
| `highLoadCluster` | Hard load concentrated over 3 consecutive days |
| `threeDayStreak` | 3+ consecutive hard days |

### 7.5 Cross-signal

`crossSignal` is set server-side when both EA and carbs are simultaneously low/high in contradictory ways. Shown as amber text below the limiter. Not a label — it is a raw pre-built string ready for display.

### 7.6 Full API response shape

```typescript
// GET /api/me/readiness/:date
{
  // Core score (from calculateSessionReadiness)
  total:            number;            // 0–100
  label:            "High" | "Moderate" | "Low" | "Poor" | "Provisional";
  primaryLimiter:   string;            // human-readable reason
  suggestedFix:     string;            // human-readable fix
  components: [                        // four items, always present
    { name: "Sleep",                score: number, maxPoints: 30, detail: string },
    { name: "Energy Availability",  score: number, maxPoints: 30, detail: string },
    { name: "Carbs",                score: number, maxPoints: 25, detail: string },
    { name: "AMQS",                 score: number, maxPoints: 15, detail: string },
  ];
  incomplete:       boolean;
  provisional:      boolean;
  missingData:      string[];          // e.g. ["sleep"]
  crossSignal:      string | null;

  // Route-added fields
  date:             string;            // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  plannedIntensity: "rest" | "light" | "moderate" | "hard";
  todayClassification: string;
  hasPlannedTraining:  boolean;
  hasYesterdayFood:    boolean;
  hasYesterdayTraining: boolean;       // always true (server treats absent = rest)
  bodyweightSource: "today" | "recent" | "profile" | null;
  bodyweightKg:     number | null;
  checkin:          ProvisionalCheckin | null;
  provisionalReadiness: {
    score:          number;
    label:          "Good" | "Moderate" | "Caution" | "Low";
    feelScore:      number;
    fuelScore:      number;
    intensityScore: number;
    message:        string;
    suggestedFix:   string;
  } | null;
  loadWarnings:         string[];
  backToBackHardDays:   boolean;
  highLoadCluster:      boolean;
  threeDayStreak:       boolean;
  yesterdayTrainingDemand: string | null;
}
```

### 7.7 Frontend rendering (`SessionReadiness.tsx`)

Query: `["/api/me/readiness", date]` → `GET /api/me/readiness/${date}`

**Display values (provisional takes priority when both provisional=true AND provisionalReadiness is present):**
```
displayScore  = provisional && pr ? pr.score : data.total
displayLabel  = provisional && pr ? pr.label : data.label
displayFix    = provisional && pr ? pr.suggestedFix : data.suggestedFix
displayLimiter = provisional && pr ? pr.message : data.primaryLimiter
```

**Badge:** `{displayScore} — {displayLabel}` (shows `~{score}` when provisional)

**Progress bar:** value = `displayScore` (0–100), color class from label:
```
High → [&>div]:bg-green-400
Moderate → [&>div]:bg-yellow-400
Low → [&>div]:bg-orange-400
Poor → [&>div]:bg-red-400
Provisional → [&>div]:bg-blue-300
```

**Conditional elements (all logic from API response, no frontend calculation):**
- `data.provisional` → show blue info box (data-testid="notice-provisional")
- `data.crossSignal` (and not provisional) → amber text below limiter (data-testid="text-cross-signal")
- `data.backToBackHardDays || data.highLoadCluster || data.threeDayStreak` (and not provisional) → orange load stacking warning (data-testid="text-load-stacking")
  - threeDayStreak → "Three consecutive high-load days — consider recovery support"
  - highLoadCluster → "Training load is clustering across consecutive days"
  - backToBackHardDays → "Back-to-back hard training days — recovery demand is elevated"
- `!data.hasPlannedTraining` → italic muted note: "No training session planned — using moderate defaults"

**Collapsible details section:**
- Provisional + provisionalReadiness: shows Wellness / Perceived fueling / Session demand sub-scores
- Objective: shows `data.components` breakdown with `score/maxPoints` and `detail` string
- Footer footnote: bodyweightKg + bodyweightSource if present

**data-testids:**
- `card-session-readiness`
- `badge-readiness-label`
- `progress-readiness`
- `notice-provisional`
- `text-primary-limiter`
- `text-suggested-fix`
- `text-cross-signal`
- `text-load-stacking`
- `button-readiness-details` (collapsible trigger)

---

## 8. Fuel Availability & Glycogen Risk

> ⚠️ **ALL calculations happen on the server.** The frontend (`FuelAvailability.tsx`) is pure display — render the API response directly. Do NOT re-implement EA or glycogen thresholds in the mobile client.

### 8.1 Endpoint

```
GET /api/me/fuel/:date        (date = YYYY-MM-DD)
```

### 8.2 How it is computed (server-side)

Uses yesterday's food + training data alongside today's planned load.

#### Fuel Status

```
FFM (kg) = bodyweightKg × (1 − bodyFatPct)   [default bodyFatPct = 0.15]
EA       = (caloriesYesterday − exerciseKcalYesterday) / FFM
```

| EA | fuelStatus |
|---|---|
| ≥ 40 kcal/kg FFM | "High" |
| ≥ 30 | "Adequate" |
| < 30 | "Low" |

If bodyweight is unavailable: fuelStatus = "Adequate" (fallback).

#### Glycogen Risk

```
carbsPerKg = carbsYesterdayG / bodyweightKg
```

Compared against thresholds that vary by today's `plannedIntensity`:

| Intensity | High risk if | Moderate risk if | Low risk if |
|---|---|---|---|
| hard | carbsPerKg < 4 | 4–6 | > 6 |
| moderate | < 3.5 | 3.5–5 | > 5 |
| light / rest | < 2.5 | 2.5–4 | > 4 |

If bodyweight unavailable: glycogenRisk = "Moderate" (fallback).

#### `plannedIntensity` derivation (server-side)

1. If today has sessions with activities → use `computeDailyLoad()` classification mapped to "light" / "moderate" / "hard"
2. If today has sessions but no activities → use session `intensity` field (vigorous → hard)
3. If no sessions → "moderate" (default)

#### `constraint` and `suggestedFix` strings

These are fully pre-built on the server. Priority order:
1. glycogenRisk = "High" → constraint describes deficit; suggestedFix gives carb amounts
2. fuelStatus = "Low" → constraint = "Overall energy intake was low yesterday"
3. glycogenRisk = "Moderate" → "+40–60g carbs pre-session…"
4. else → "Fuel stores look adequate" / "Fuel looks good — stay hydrated…"

#### Provisional mode

`provisional = !hasYesterdayFood` (missing yesterday food triggers provisional; training absence is assumed rest).

When provisional AND ProvisionalCheckin exists, the server computes `provisionalFuel` from `calculateProvisionalFuel(fueledToday, plannedIntensity)`:

| fueledToday | plannedIntensity | fuelStatus | fuelRisk |
|---|---|---|---|
| "yes" | any | "Adequate" | "Low" |
| "somewhat" | "hard" | "Low" | "Elevated" |
| "somewhat" | other | "Adequate" | "Elevated" |
| "no" | "hard" | "Low" | "Elevated" |
| "no" | other | "Low" | "Elevated" |

Note: provisional fuel status is capped at "Adequate" — "High" requires objective food log data.

In provisional mode, the UI shows **Fuel Availability Risk** (from `provisionalFuel.fuelRisk`: Low / Elevated / Unclear) instead of Glycogen Risk.

#### Load stacking + fuelLoadWarning

Same `computeLoadWarnings()` logic as readiness. `fuelLoadWarning` string is set when:
- stacking detected AND (glycogenRisk = High or Moderate) → "Training demand is stacking while fuel support is low"
- today is hard/very_hard AND glycogenRisk = High → "High training demand with low carbohydrate support"

### 8.3 Full API response shape

```typescript
// GET /api/me/fuel/:date
{
  // From calculateFuelAvailability
  fuelStatus:    "High" | "Adequate" | "Low";
  glycogenRisk:  "Low" | "Moderate" | "High";
  constraint:    string;           // pre-built by server
  suggestedFix:  string;           // pre-built by server
  eaValue:       number | null;    // kcal/kg FFM, rounded to 1dp
  carbsPerKg:    number | null;    // g/kg, rounded to 1dp
  ffmKg:         number | null;

  // Route-added fields
  date:              string;
  plannedIntensity:  "rest" | "light" | "moderate" | "hard";
  hasPlannedTraining: boolean;
  bodyweightSource:  "today" | "recent" | "profile" | null;
  bodyweightKg:      number | null;
  provisional:       boolean;
  hasYesterdayFood:  boolean;
  hasYesterdayTraining: boolean;   // always true
  checkin:           ProvisionalCheckin | null;
  provisionalFuel: {
    fuelStatus:  "Adequate" | "Low";
    fuelRisk:    "Low" | "Elevated" | "Unclear";
    message:     string;
    suggestedFix: string;
  } | null;
  fuelLoadWarning:     string | null;
  backToBackHardDays:  boolean;
  highLoadCluster:     boolean;
  threeDayStreak:      boolean;
  yesterdayTrainingDemand: string | null;
}
```

### 8.4 Frontend rendering (`FuelAvailability.tsx`)

Query: `["/api/me/fuel", date]` → `GET /api/me/fuel/${date}`

**Display values (provisional with check-in takes priority):**
```
isProvisionalWithCheckin = data.provisional && !!data.provisionalFuel
displayFuelStatus = isProvisionalWithCheckin ? provisionalFuel.fuelStatus : data.fuelStatus
displayFix        = isProvisionalWithCheckin ? provisionalFuel.suggestedFix : data.suggestedFix
```

**Fuel Status badge colors:**
```
High / Adequate → text-green-400 border-green-400/30 bg-green-400/10
Low             → text-red-400 border-red-400/30 bg-red-400/10
```
When `provisional && !provisionalFuel` → badge shows "Provisional" in blue.

**Glycogen Risk row (or Fuel Availability Risk in provisional mode):**
```
Glycogen Risk badge colors:
  Low      → green
  Moderate → yellow
  High     → red

Fuel Availability Risk badge colors (provisional):
  Low      → green
  Elevated → yellow
  Unclear  → muted/secondary
```

**Conditional elements:**
- `data.provisional` → blue info box (data-testid="notice-fuel-provisional")
- `showObjectiveWarning` (= !provisional && (fuelStatus=Low || glycogenRisk=High)) → orange warning block with `data.constraint` (data-testid="text-fuel-constraint")
- `!data.provisional && data.fuelLoadWarning` → orange text (data-testid="text-fuel-load-warning")
- Always shown: Zap icon + `displayFix` (data-testid="text-fuel-fix")
- Footer metrics row (only when `!provisional && eaValue !== null && carbsPerKg !== null`):
  `EA: {eaValue} kcal/kg   Carbs: {carbsPerKg} g/kg   Intensity: {plannedIntensity}`

**data-testids:**
- `card-fuel-availability`
- `badge-fuel-status`
- `badge-glycogen-risk`
- `notice-fuel-provisional`
- `text-provisional-fuel-message`
- `text-fuel-constraint`
- `text-fuel-load-warning`
- `text-fuel-fix`

---

## 8.5 Provisional Check-In Card

The Provisional Check-In card is a self-report form that appears on the dashboard **only when readiness data is incomplete** (sleep not logged). It feeds answers directly into the server's provisional readiness and provisional fuel calculations documented in §7.3 and §8.2.

> The card does **no calculations itself.** It collects three (or four) answers, saves them via `PUT /api/me/provisional-checkin/:date`, then invalidates the readiness and fuel queries — causing both `SessionReadiness.tsx` and `FuelAvailability.tsx` to re-fetch and display provisional estimates computed entirely on the server.

### 8.5.1 When it renders

The component (`ProvisionalCheckIn.tsx`) is always mounted in the dashboard at position 7 in the component order (after `ReadinessSummaryCard`). However, it **returns null** unless `readiness.provisional === true`, which is driven by `GET /api/me/readiness/:date` → `provisional` field.

```typescript
// ProvisionalCheckIn.tsx — gate logic
if (!readiness?.provisional) return null;
```

So the card is invisible when all data is present. No extra gate component is needed.

### 8.5.2 Database table

`provisional_checkins` — unique per `(userId, date)`. Upsert on every submission.

```typescript
{
  id:                        number;
  userId:                    number;
  date:                      string;            // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  feelToday:                 "fresh" | "okay" | "tired";
  fueledToday:               "yes" | "somewhat" | "no";
  plannedIntensity:          "light" | "moderate" | "hard";
  trainedYesterday:          boolean | null;    // null = question not shown
  yesterdayTrainingIntensity: "light" | "moderate" | "hard" | null;
  createdAt:                 Date;
  updatedAt:                 Date;
}
```

### 8.5.3 API endpoints

```
GET /api/me/provisional-checkin/:date
  → ProvisionalCheckin | null

PUT /api/me/provisional-checkin/:date
  Body: {
    feelToday:                  "fresh" | "okay" | "tired",
    fueledToday:                "yes" | "somewhat" | "no",
    plannedIntensity:           "light" | "moderate" | "hard",
    trainedYesterday?:          boolean | null,
    yesterdayTrainingIntensity?: "light" | "moderate" | "hard" | null,
  }
  → Upserted ProvisionalCheckin

Cache invalidations on successful PUT:
  ["/api/me/readiness", date]
  ["/api/me/fuel", date]
```

The PUT uses upsert logic (update if exists for that userId+date, insert otherwise). The frontend never calls GET directly — it reads `checkin` from the embedded field in `GET /api/me/readiness/:date`.

### 8.5.4 Questions and options

Three questions are always shown. A fourth (yesterday's training) appears conditionally.

| # | Question text | Field | Options |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | "How do you feel today?" | `feelToday` | 💪 Fresh / 😐 Okay / 😴 Tired |
| 2 | "Did you fuel well yesterday?" | `fueledToday` | 🟢 Yes / 🟡 Somewhat / 🔴 Not really |
| 3 | "Planned session intensity" | `plannedIntensity` | 🚶 Light / 🏃 Moderate / 🔥 Hard |
| 4 (conditional) | "Did you train yesterday?" | `trainedYesterday` | ✅ Yes / 😴 No / Rest |

**Q4 appears only when** `!readiness.hasYesterdayTraining`. In practice `hasYesterdayTraining` is currently always `true` on the server (absent sessions = treated as rest), so this question is rarely shown. If Q4 = Yes, a follow-up row appears: "How hard was yesterday's session?" → `yesterdayTrainingIntensity` (same Light / Moderate / Hard options).

The question count shown in the subtitle: `3 questions` or `4 questions — drives estimated readiness & fuel status`.

### 8.5.5 Toggle button styling

Each answer is a full-width `<button>` inside a `flex gap-2` row. Selected vs unselected:

```
Selected:   border-primary bg-primary/10 text-primary font-semibold
Unselected: border-border/40 bg-secondary/20 text-muted-foreground
            hover: hover:border-border hover:bg-secondary/40
```

Button inner layout: `flex flex-col items-center gap-1 py-2.5 px-1 rounded-lg text-xs border transition-all`
- Top: `<span className="text-lg leading-none">` emoji
- Bottom: `<span>` label text

### 8.5.6 Submit state and validation

Submit button is disabled until the three core questions are answered (`feelToday && fueledToday && plannedIntensity`). If Q4 is visible, `trainedYesterday !== null` is also required.

Button label: `"Submit check-in"` (pending: `"Saving…"`) on first submit; `"Update"` (pending: `"Saving…"`) when editing an existing check-in.

### 8.5.7 Completed state (read-only summary)

After a successful submission, the card switches to a compact summary view showing all three answers as a 3-column grid of emoji + label cards:

```
┌────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┐
│  💪         │  🟢          │  🏃           │
│  Feeling   │  Fueled     │  Today's plan│
│  Fresh     │  Yes        │  Moderate    │
└────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┘
```

Header: CheckCircle2 icon + "Quick Check-in" title + blue "Estimated" badge + pencil edit button.

If `trainedYesterday !== null`: a text row below the grid shows:
- Yes + intensity → `"✅ Trained yesterday — {intensity}"`
- No → `"😴 Rest day yesterday"`

Footer disclaimer: `"Readiness and fuel status are estimated from your self-report — not objective data. Log yesterday's food and training for a complete assessment."` (text-[10px] italic muted)

Edit button (`data-testid="button-edit-checkin"`) re-opens the form pre-populated with existing answers.

### 8.5.8 data-testids

| Element | data-testid |
|---|---|
| Card (both states) | `card-provisional-checkin` |
| Toggle: feel-today options | `toggle-feel-{fresh\|okay\|tired}` |
| Toggle: fueled-today options | `toggle-fuel-{yes\|somewhat\|no}` |
| Toggle: planned intensity options | `toggle-intensity-{light\|moderate\|hard}` |
| Toggle: trained yesterday | `toggle-trained-yesterday-{true\|false}` |
| Toggle: yesterday intensity | `toggle-yesterday-intensity-{light\|moderate\|hard}` |
| Submit / Update button | `button-submit-checkin` |
| Cancel button (edit mode) | `button-cancel-checkin` |
| Edit (pencil) button | `button-edit-checkin` |
| Question labels | `label-feel-today`, `label-fueled-today`, `label-planned-intensity`, `label-trained-yesterday` |

### 8.5.9 Dashboard position

```
[dashboard component order]
5.  <MorningCheckIn date={selectedDate} />
6.  <ReadinessSummaryCard date={selectedDate} />   ← compact readiness chip row
7.  <ProvisionalCheckIn date={selectedDate} />     ← this card (hidden when not provisional)
8.  Daily Intake Estimates card
```

The card sits **below** the readiness summary but **above** the macro targets. This order is important: the user sees the provisional score in position 6, then immediately sees the check-in prompt in position 7 that drives it.

---

## 8.6 Morning Check-In — "Start Your Day" Dialog & Dashboard Card

Two components implement the morning check-in flow. They share the same API and data model but appear in different contexts:

| Component | File | Where rendered | Trigger |
|---|---|---|---|
| `MorningCheckInGate` | `MorningCheckInGate.tsx` | Global, outside Router (`App.tsx`) | On every page load when gate not yet dismissed today |
| `MorningCheckIn` | `MorningCheckIn.tsx` | Dashboard, slot 5 | Always mounted — self-hides when all 3 items done |

---

### 8.6.1 API endpoints

#### `GET /api/me/morning-status/:date`
The primary status query used by both components. All server-side — no frontend computation.

```typescript
// Response shape
{
  hasSleep:           boolean;       // sleep log exists for :date
  hasWeight:          boolean;       // ≥1 weight entry exists for :date
  hasPlannedTraining: boolean;       // ≥1 workout session exists for :date
  isRestDay:          boolean;       // rest day marked AND no sessions
  sleepLog:           { hoursSlept: number; sleepQuality: number | null } | null;
  weightLog:          { weight: number } | null;
}
```

`isRestDay` logic: `isRestDayMarked && sessions.length === 0` — a logged training session overrides the rest-day mark.

#### `PUT /api/me/sleep/:date`
Upsert sleep log. Body: `{ hoursSlept: number (0–24), sleepQuality?: number | null (1–5) }`. Returns the upserted log.

#### `GET /api/me/sleep/:date`
Returns sleep log for date or `null`.

#### `POST /api/me/rest-day/:date`
Marks the date as a rest day. Returns `{ isRestDay: true }`.

#### `DELETE /api/me/rest-day/:date`
Removes the rest-day mark. Returns `{ isRestDay: false }`.

#### `POST /api/weights`
Log morning weight. Body: `{ date: string, weight: number }`.

---

### 8.6.2 Gate visibility logic — `useMorningCheckInGate`

> 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE only.** No server logic — reads `morning-status` and `localStorage`.

**File:** `client/src/hooks/useMorningCheckInGate.ts`

**localStorage key:** `checkInGateSeen:{YYYY-MM-DD}` — one key per calendar day.

**`shouldShow` conditions — ALL must be true:**
1. User is authenticated (`/api/user/me` returns a user)
2. User is onboarded (`user.targetCalories != null`)
3. Gate not yet seen today (`localStorage.getItem(storageKey) !== "true"` AND `markedSeen === false`)
4. `morning-status` response has loaded (`!!status`)
5. Not all done (`!allDone`)

**`allDone`:** `hasSleep && hasWeight && hasPlannedTraining`

The status query is only enabled when `isAuthenticated && isOnboarded && !alreadySeen`. So if the gate has already been dismissed, no network request is made.

**`markSeen()`:** `localStorage.setItem(storageKey, "true")` + sets `markedSeen = true` in state.

**Auto-complete detection:** A `useEffect` in `MorningCheckInGate` watches `allDone`. When it goes true while the gate was previously open (`gateWasOpen.current === true`), `markSeen()` is called automatically and a toast fires: `"Check-in complete — your targets are up to date"`.

---

### 8.6.3 MorningCheckInGate — "Start your day" dialog

**Mounted in `App.tsx`** as `<GatedMorningCheckIn>` — a thin wrapper that returns `null` when `location.startsWith("/onboarding")`, otherwise renders `<MorningCheckInGate>`. This means the dialog can appear on ANY authenticated page except during onboarding.

```typescript
// App.tsx mounting
function GatedMorningCheckIn() {
  const [location] = useLocation();
  if (location.startsWith("/onboarding")) return null;
  return <MorningCheckInGate />;
}

// Inside App():
<QueryClientProvider ...>
  <Router />
  <GatedMorningCheckIn />   ← outside the Router, renders on every page
</QueryClientProvider>
```

#### Dialog structure

```
Dialog open={shouldShow}
  onOpenChange: backdrop/Escape → handleContinue()

  className="max-w-sm w-[calc(100%-2rem)] rounded-xl p-0 gap-0 overflow-hidden"

Inner div className="p-5 space-y-4"
  DialogHeader (space-y-1):
    DialogTitle:   "Start your day"               (font-display text-base font-semibold)
    DialogDescription: "Complete your check-in to get accurate readiness and fuel targets"

  [optional] Incomplete notice (text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center leading-relaxed)
```


The training row is never in a "form expanded" state — it navigates to the training page.

#### handleContinue behaviour

```typescript
function handleContinue() {
  markSeen();
  if (!allDone) {
    toast({ title: "You can complete your check-in anytime from the dashboard" });
  }
}
```
Called by both the Continue button and the dialog's `onOpenChange` (backdrop / Escape).

### 8.6.4 MorningCheckIn — inline dashboard card

### 8.6.5 Key differences between the two components

| | Gate dialog (`MorningCheckInGate`) | Dashboard card (`MorningCheckIn`) |
|---|---|---|
| Trigger | Once per day on any page load (unless dismissed) | Always mounted on dashboard — self-hides when done |
| Training satisfied by | `hasPlannedTraining` only | `hasPlannedTraining` OR `isRestDay` |
| Training action | "Add" button → navigates to `/training` | "Mark as rest day" button (POST rest-day API) |
| Dismiss path | Continue button or backdrop/Escape | Auto-disappears when all 3 done |
| Sleep already logged | Shows "Sleep logged" + check (no edit) | Shows editable "tap to edit" row |
| Weight already logged | Shows "Weight logged" + check (no edit) | Shows editable "tap to edit" row |
| Persistence | `localStorage` gate per day | No separate persistence — reads from API status |
| Sleep form `autoFocus` | Yes | No |

## 9. Weight-Cut Engine

### 9.0 Server vs Client responsibility — quick reference

> **Read this first.** The replicating agent does not need to re-implement any nutrition math or weight-cut planning math on the frontend. All of that lives on the server and is delivered as pre-computed fields in API responses.

| What | Where | How the frontend gets it |
|---|---|---|
| `calculateWeightCutPlan()` — daysUntil, weeklyRate, weeklyTargets, status, suggestedDeficitKcal, fatLossRequired, tempCut | **Server** (`server/lib/weight-cut.ts`) | Returned directly by `GET /api/me/weight-cut` |
| Calorie target, protein, carbs, fat for the day | **Server** (`GET /api/me/targets/effective`) | Read from API response — frontend renders only |
| EA value, `isLowEA`, `eaRecommendedCalories` | **Server** (`GET /api/me/targets/effective`) | Read from API response |
| Carb flags, `isLowCarb`, `carbRecommendedG` | **Server** (`GET /api/me/targets/effective`) | Read from API response |
| Day type classification (hard / very_hard / moderate / light / rest) | **Server** (`computeDailyLoad`) | Returned as `dayType` in effective-targets response |
| BMR, TDEE, planned deficit | **Server** | Returned as `baselineTdee`, `dailyDeficit`, `tdee` |
| Status badge colour map | **Client** (`WeightCutHero.tsx`) | Local lookup object — safe to replicate as a constant |
| Pace badge label (`getPaceInfo`) | **Client** (`WeightCutHero.tsx`) | Pure display function — uses `weeklyRatePct` from API |
| Trend message (`getTrendMessage`) | **Client** (`WeightCutHero.tsx`) | Pure display function — uses weight history from API |
| Consistency label (`getConsistencyLabel`) | **Client** (`WeightCutHero.tsx`) | Pure display function — uses count derived from API data |
| Consent decisions (EA / carb accepted / declined) | **Client** (`localStorage` via `useFightCampOverride`) | Never touches the server — client state only |
| Override calorie/carb values after user accepts | **Client** (`useFightCampOverride`) | Applied in dashboard `useMemo` on top of server values |
| `projectedCut` chart data for share-moment after plan creation | **Client** (`WeightCutHero.tsx`) | Locally approximated from form values — share-card animation only, not used for any nutrition logic |

**Rule of thumb:** If a number appears in the effective-targets or weight-cut API response, the frontend must not recompute it — just read the field.

---

Defined in `server/lib/weight-cut.ts` — **pure functions, no side effects, called server-side only**.

### 9.1 Two flows: `same_day` vs `day_before`

**same_day** — athlete competes on the same day as weigh-in:
- All weight loss must come from sustainable fat loss (1% BW/week cap)
- No water manipulation window available
- Harder: requires longer run-up

**day_before** — athlete weighs in the day before competing:
- Allows temporary water/glycogen reduction in the final 24–48h
- Fat loss component handles the structural deficit
- Temp cut component handles the final flush

### 9.2 `calculateWeightCutPlan(inputs)` — main entry point

> 🖥️ **SERVER-SIDE ONLY.** Called inside `GET /api/me/weight-cut` and `GET /api/me/targets/effective`. The frontend never imports or calls this function — it reads the pre-computed fields from the API response.

Inputs:
```typescript
{
  currentWeight: number   // kg
  targetWeight: number    // kg
  fightDate: string       // YYYY-MM-DD
  weighInTiming: 'same_day' | 'day_before'
  manualTempReductionKg?: number  // override auto-calc of water cut portion
}
```

Returns:
```typescript
{
  totalDrop: number             // kg to lose
  fatLossDrop: number           // kg via fat loss
  tempCutDrop: number           // kg via water/glycogen (day_before only)
  weeksAvailable: number
  recommendedWeeklyRate: number // kg/week fat loss
  isAchievable: boolean
  status: CutStatus  // 'on_track'|'aggressive'|'very_aggressive'|'unrealistic'|'complete'|'past_date'
  weeklyTargets: WeeklyTarget[] // for chart
  warnings: string[]
}
```

### 9.3 `buildWeeklyTargets()`

> 🖥️ **SERVER-SIDE ONLY.** Called inside `GET /api/me/weight-cut`. The `weeklyTargets` array is returned in the response and rendered directly by the frontend — the frontend does not compute it.

Produces an array of `{ week, projectedWeight, caloricDeficitPerDay }` for the weight trend chart on the dashboard and in ShareMomentSheet.

### 9.4 Constraints
  - Max sustainable fat loss: 1% of body weight per week (hard cap)
  - Temp cut capped at 5–8% body weight (adjustable by `manualTempReductionKg`)
  - Risk/status is driven by `requiredWeeklyRatePct` — the % of current bodyweight that must be lost per week to reach target in time. It is **not** an absolute kg threshold (a 90 kg athlete has a higher cap than a 55 kg one):

  | requiredWeeklyRatePct | CutStatus | Label shown to user |
  |---|---|---|
  | ≤ 0.5% BW/wk | `on_track` | "Steady pace" |
  | ≤ 1.0% BW/wk | `on_track` | "On track" |
  | ≤ 1.5% BW/wk | `aggressive` | "Quite aggressive — consider extending timeline" |
  | ≤ 2.0% BW/wk | `very_aggressive` | "Very aggressive — adjust target or date" |
  | > 2.0% BW/wk | `unrealistic` | "Unrealistic — not achievable safely" |

  **Pace badge** on `WeightCutHero` uses the *recommended* rate (capped at 1% BW/wk via `getPaceInfo(weeklyRatePct)`):
  - < 0.5% → "Easy pace" (muted grey)
  - ≤ 0.75% → "Moderate pace" (orange)
  - > 0.75% → "Aggressive pace" (yellow)

  Full `CutStatus` type: `"on_track" | "aggressive" | "very_aggressive" | "unrealistic" | "complete" | "past_date"`

---

### 9.5 API endpoints

#### `GET /api/me/weight-cut`
Returns the current plan enriched with live calculations. Body weight is resolved via `resolveBodyweight()` (latest logged weight → profile weight → 75 kg fallback; source is returned as `bodyweightSource`).

Response shape:
```typescript
{
  planId:                number;
  currentWeight:         number;         // kg — resolved live bodyweight
  targetWeight:          number;         // kg — from plan record
  fightDate:             string;         // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  daysUntil:             number;
  weeksUntil:            number;
  totalToLose:           number;         // totalDrop from calculateWeightCutPlan
  fatLossRequired:       number;         // fatLossDrop
  tempCut:               number;         // tempCutDrop (auto)
  tempCutDisplayed:      number;         // what we show (may differ from tempCut if manual override)
  weeklyRate:            number;         // kg/wk fat loss pace
  weeklyRatePct:         number;         // % BW/wk
  dayMinus4Target:       number | null;  // only populated within 10 days of fight
  status:                CutStatus;
  statusLabel:           string;
  weeklyTargets:         Array<{ week: number; targetWeight: number }>;
  suggestedDeficitKcal:  number;
  bodyweightSource:      string;
  weighInTiming:         "same_day" | "day_before";
  manualTempReductionKg: number | null;
}
```

#### `POST /api/me/weight-cut`
**Create or replace** — deletes any existing plan first, then inserts a new one. Used for both initial creation AND the "Update Plan" action from the edit modal in `WeightCutHero`.

Request body:
```typescript
{
  currentWeight:         number;    // required
  targetWeight:          number;    // required
  fightDate:             string;    // required, "YYYY-MM-DD"
  weighInTiming?:        "same_day" | "day_before";   // default "same_day"
  manualTempReductionKg?: number | null;
}
```
Returns 201 with the same shape as GET.

#### `PUT /api/me/weight-cut`
Partial update — patches fields on the existing plan without deleting it. Returns 404 if no plan exists.

#### `DELETE /api/me/weight-cut`
Deletes the plan. Returns 200 `{ ok: true }`.

> **Important:** `WeightCutHero` always uses `POST` for both create and edit (replace-then-create). The `PUT` endpoint exists for partial-patch callers (e.g. future automated updates).

#### `GET /api/me/targets/effective`
Fight-camp-aware effective targets. Accepts optional `?date=YYYY-MM-DD`. Full shape documented in §9.8.

---

### 9.6 WeightCutHero — dashboard hero card

**Component:** `client/src/components/WeightCutHero.tsx`
**Mounted at:** dashboard component slot 4 — always first in the feed when a plan is active.
**Visibility:** always mounted; renders an empty state (no plan) or full hero (plan active).

#### 9.6.1 Render states

**Loading skeleton** (`data-testid="card-weight-cut-hero"`):
```
animate-pulse, three rounded lines (1/3, 1/2, 3/4 width)
```

**Empty state** (`data-testid="card-weight-cut-hero-empty"`):

```
Target icon + "Fight Camp" heading
Subtitle: "Set a fight date to start your camp plan — track your cut and stay on pace."
"Set a fight date" button (data-testid="button-create-cut-plan")
```

**Active plan** (`data-testid="card-weight-cut-hero"`, `className="border-border/50"`):

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  🎯 Fight Camp                    [status badge]  ✏️ 🗑️  │
│                                                     │
│  📅  73 days  to fight night                        │
│                                                     │

│   OR weight input form (if tapped)                   │
│   OR nothing (if already logged)                     │
│                                                     │
│  ┌──────────┬────────────────┬──────────┐           │
│  │ 77.2     │ ↓              │ 72.0     │           │
│  │ Current  │ 5.2 kg to go  │ Fight wt │           │
│  │ kg       │ 0.71 kg/wk    │          │           │
│  └──────────┴────────────────┴──────────┘           │
│                                                     │
│  [Moderate pace]          (tap → Plan breakdown)    │
│                                                     │
│  This week's target: 76.5 kg · ~500 kcal deficit    │
│                                                     │
│  🔥 On trend ↓  /  ⚡ Weight naturally fluctuates   │
│  Weight logged: 5 of last 7 days   [Building rhythm]│
│                                                     │
│  [Share icon]  Try sharing a moment                 │
│  [disclaimer text]                                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 9.6.2 Inline weight logging

Tapping the "Log today's weight" CTA (`data-testid="button-prompt-weight-hero"`) expands an inline form (`data-testid="hero-weight-input-form"`):

```
Scale icon + "Morning weight (kg)" label
Input (type=number, step=0.1, min=20, max=300, data-testid="input-hero-weight")
[Save] (data-testid="button-submit-hero-weight") + [Cancel] buttons
```

After submit, `weightMutation` fires `POST /api/weights`. On success:
- Closes form, sets `justLogged=true` for 2500 ms (green flash on current-weight cell, week-target, trend line)
- Invalidates: `["/api/me/weight-cut"]`, `["/api/me/weights/range"]`, `["/api/weights/range"]`, `["/api/me/morning-status"]`, `["/api/me/readiness"]`, `["/api/me/fuel"]`
- Fires an `fcModal` notification (see §9.12): "On trend ↓" or "Weight naturally fluctuates" (amber) if new weight > prior reading

#### 9.6.3 Status badge colours

> 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE only.** A local constant lookup — no API call needed. `status` string comes from `GET /api/me/weight-cut`.

```typescript
const statusColors = {
  on_track:       "text-green-400 border-green-400/30 bg-green-400/10",
  aggressive:     "text-yellow-400 border-yellow-400/30 bg-yellow-400/10",
  very_aggressive:"text-orange-400 border-orange-400/30 bg-orange-400/10",
  unrealistic:    "text-red-400 border-red-400/30 bg-red-400/10",
  complete:       "text-green-400 border-green-400/30 bg-green-400/10",
  past_date:      "text-muted-foreground border-border bg-secondary/20",
};
```

#### 9.6.4 Pace badge (uses recommended capped rate)

> 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE only.** Pure display function. `weeklyRatePct` comes from `GET /api/me/weight-cut` — no recalculation needed.

```typescript
function getPaceInfo(weeklyRatePct) {
  if (weeklyRatePct < 0.5)  → "Easy pace"       (muted grey)
  if (weeklyRatePct <= 0.75)→ "Moderate pace"   (text-primary)
  else                       → "Aggressive pace" (text-orange-400) + note
}
```
Displayed in `Badge variant="outline"` — tapping this row opens the Plan Breakdown dialog.

#### 9.6.5 Trend message (7-day weights)

> 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE only.** Pure display function. Weight history comes from `GET /api/me/weights/range` — the client computes only the display string, not any nutritional values.

Uses `useWeightsRange(sevenDayStart, today)` (7-day window). Logic:

```typescript
function getTrendMessage(weights, status) {
  if weights.length < 2 → "Trend forming — keep logging daily"
  if status === "complete" → "At fight weight — well done"
  if status === "past_date" → "Fight date passed"
  if change < -0.2 → "On trend — moving in the right direction"
  if -0.2 ≤ change ≤ 0.3 → "Fluctuations are normal — trends take time"
  else → "Weight naturally fluctuates — stay consistent" (isUp = true → amber)
}
```

`isUp=true` → amber `TrendingUp` icon; otherwise `Flame` icon in `text-primary/60`.

#### 9.6.6 Consistency label (7-day logging count)

> 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE only.** Pure display function. Count is derived client-side by counting unique dates in the weights range response — no server computation needed.

```typescript
function getConsistencyLabel(count) {
  if count >= 6 → { label: "Great momentum",  color: text-green-400 … }
  if count >= 4 → { label: "Building rhythm",  color: text-yellow-400 … }
  if count >= 2 → { label: "Getting started",  color: text-muted-foreground … }
  else          → null (badge not shown)
}
```

#### 9.6.7 Consistency milestone fcModals

When `consistencyCount` increases past a threshold, a fight-camp notification fires automatically:

| Threshold crossed | Modal title | Celebration |
|---|---|---|
| 3 | "Building rhythm 🔥" | `fireCelebration("🔥")` |
| 5 | "Great momentum 🥊" | `fireCelebration("🥊")` |
| 6 | "Excellent 💪" | `fireCelebration("💪")` |

These only fire when `!weightWentUpRef.current` (i.e. the new weight was not higher than prior).

#### 9.6.8 Fat loss breakdown dialog

Tapping the pace badge row (anywhere on the `button-open-breakdown` button) opens a `Dialog` (`max-w-sm mx-4`):

```
Title: "Plan breakdown"  Desc: "How your weight cut is structured."
─────────────────────────────────────────────────
Fat loss target         | {fatLossRequired} kg     (data-testid="text-fat-loss-required")
Temporary reduction     | ~{tempCutDisplayed} kg   (data-testid="text-temp-cut")
  OR "Estimated temp."  | ~{tempCut} kg  (if tempCutDisplayed == 0 but tempCut > 0)
Target by D−4 (≤10d)    | ≤ {dayMinus4Target} kg  (data-testid="text-day-minus4-target")
─────────────────────────────────────────────────
Fat-loss pace           | [Pace badge] + note      (data-testid="text-pace-note")
Daily deficit target    | ~{suggestedDeficitKcal} kcal
```

D−4 row only visible when `plan.dayMinus4Target !== null && plan.daysUntil <= 10`.
`tempCutDisplayed` row takes priority over `tempCut` row; if both are zero, neither renders.

**Lives inside `WeightCutHero`** (the `formDialog` const, rendered at the bottom of both empty and active card branches). Both `openCreate()` and `openEdit()` open the same dialog — only `dialogMode` changes the title, description, and submit button label.

#### 9.7.5 Submit behaviour

`handleSubmit()` calls `createMutation.mutate(...)` in both create and edit modes. The `POST /api/me/weight-cut` endpoint deletes any existing plan and inserts a new one.

**On success (create mode):**
- `fireCelebration("🎯")`
- Queues `fcModal` with `chartType: "fight_camp_new"` + projected cut data
  > 💻 **CLIENT-SIDE approximation** — `projectedCut` is locally estimated from form values (`currentWeight`, `targetWeight`, `fightDate`) purely for the share-card chart animation. It is **not** the authoritative weekly targets. The server's `weeklyTargets` (from `GET /api/me/weight-cut`) are the real values used everywhere else.
- Title: "Fight camp set 🎯" + "{N} week(s) to make weight. Let's get to work."

**On success (edit mode):**
- `toast({ title: "Fight camp plan updated 🎯" })`
- No fcModal queued

Both invalidate `["/api/me/weight-cut"]`.

### 9.8 Fight Camp Calorie Model — `GET /api/me/targets/effective`

> 🖥️ **ENTIRELY SERVER-SIDE.** The frontend **must not** replicate any of the formulas below. It calls `GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD` and renders the pre-computed response fields directly. The only client-side work is applying the user's consent overrides from `useFightCampOverride` (§9.9) on top of the returned values.

When a fight camp plan is active and `daysUntil > 0`, the effective-targets endpoint enters fight camp mode. This is the **single source of truth** for all macro targets shown on the dashboard.

**Priority:** Fight Camp Active > Profile Goal > Maintenance default.

#### Formula (server-side, for reference only)

```
1. tdeeNoExercise = bmr × 1.4              (NEAT only, no structured exercise)
2. exerciseKcalRaw = Σ session.estimatedKcal for targetDate
   exerciseKcalAdjusted = exerciseKcalRaw   (alias)
3. exerciseKcalAddedBack = round(exerciseKcalAdjusted × 0.8)
   → only 80% of training kcal added back (built-in deficit buffer)
4. plannedDeficitKcal = round(cut.recommendedWeeklyRate × 7700 / 7)
5. plannedCalories = round(tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAddedBack − plannedDeficitKcal)
6. targetCalories = plannedCalories   (NO floor clamping — user decides via modals)
```

#### Macro split by day type

Day type comes from `computeDailyLoad(activities, sessionCount).classification`:

| dayType | Protein (g/kg) | Fat (g/kg) |
|---|---|---|
| `hard` | 1.8 | 0.7 |
| `very_hard` | 1.8 | 0.5 |
| `moderate` | 2.0 | 0.9 |
| `light` | 2.0 | 0.9 |
| rest day | 2.0 | 1.0 |

Carbs absorb the residual: `targetCarbs = max(0, targetCalories − protein×4 − fat×9) / 4`

Body fat % defaults to 15% if not set on profile. `ffmKg = currentWeight × (1 − bodyFatPct)`.

#### EA and carb flag logic

```
eaValue = round((plannedCalories − exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg, 1)
isLowEA  = eaValue < 30

carbsPerKg = targetCarbs / currentWeight
isLowCarb  = exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0 && !isRestDay && carbsPerKg < 3
```

Carb floor only fires on training days with logged sessions (not rest days, not sessions with no kcal).

#### Recommendations

```
eaRecommendedCalories = round(exerciseKcalAdjusted + 30 × ffmKg)   // exactly hits EA=30
carbRecommendedG      = round(3 × currentWeight)                     // IOC/ISSN minimum
```

#### Soft performance warnings (toast, not modal)

| Condition | isBelowPerformanceCarb | performanceCarbWarning |
|---|---|---|
| `hard` day, carbsPerKg < 4, !isLowCarb | true | "...increasing toward ~5 g/kg..." |
| `very_hard` day, carbsPerKg < 5, !isLowCarb | true | "...increasing toward ~5–7 g/kg..." |

#### Full API response shape (fight_camp mode)

```typescript
{
  mode:                   "fight_camp",
  modeLabel:              "Fight Camp Fat Loss",
  modeNote:               string,             // "Training is included…" or "Rest day…"
  targetCalories:         number,
  targetProtein:          number,
  targetCarbs:            number,
  targetFat:              number,
  tdee:                   number,             // tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAdjusted
  baselineTdee:           number,             // tdeeNoExercise only
  trainingKcalToday:      number,             // raw (no RPE adj) — for existing consumers
  trainingKcalTodayAdjusted: number,
  trainingKcalAddedBack:  number,             // exerciseKcalAdjusted × 0.8
  exerciseAddBackPct:     0.8,
  dailyDeficit:           number,             // plannedDeficitKcal
  plannedCalories:        number,
  dayType:                DayClassification,
  ffmKg:                  number,
  eaValue:                number,
  carbsPerKg:             number,
  isLowEA:                boolean,
  isLowCarb:              boolean,
  eaRecommendedCalories:  number,
  carbRecommendedG:       number,
  isBelowPerformanceCarb: boolean,
  performanceCarbWarning: string | null,
  trainingCalorieCreditPct: 0,               // always 0 — client must NOT add exercise again
  provisional:            boolean,
  weeklyRate:             number,
  weeklyRatePct:          number,
  daysUntil:              number,
  planId:                 number,
  planFightDate:          string,
  planTargetWeight:       number,
}
```

> `trainingCalorieCreditPct: 0` is a critical flag — the dashboard must not add exercise calories on top of this target. The add-back is already baked in.

---

### 9.9 `useFightCampOverride` hook

> 💻 **ENTIRELY CLIENT-SIDE.** This hook never calls any API. It reads the server-computed `isLowEA` and `isLowCarb` flags from the effective-targets response, stores the user's decision in `localStorage`, and returns optional override values that the dashboard applies on top of the server values.

**File:** `client/src/hooks/useFightCampOverride.ts`
**Purpose:** Manages the EA and carb consent modals. Persists decisions in `localStorage` so modals never re-appear for the same plan on the same date once the user has chosen.

#### Inputs

```typescript
{
  userId:          number | undefined,
  date:            string,             // today's date ("YYYY-MM-DD")
  effectiveTargets: FightCampTargets | undefined,
  isFightCamp:     boolean,
  planFingerprint?: string,            // change-detection for plan modifications
}
```

`planFingerprint` is constructed in dashboard.tsx by combining `planId + fightDate + targetWeight`. Any change to the plan generates a new fingerprint → new storage key → modals re-trigger automatically on the new plan.

#### localStorage key format

```
fightCamp:{userId}:{date}:{planFingerprint}   // if planFingerprint present
fightCamp:{userId}:{date}                     // fallback (no fingerprint)
```

Stored value:
```typescript
{ ea?: "accepted" | "declined", carb?: "accepted" | "declined", perfToastShown?: boolean }
```

#### Auto-open logic

On mount / when `isFightCamp`, `isLowEA`, `isLowCarb`, or `storageKey` changes:
1. If `isLowEA && !stored.ea` → open EA modal
2. Else if `isLowCarb && !stored.carb` → open carb modal

Only one modal opens at a time. The carb modal is chained after the EA modal closes (350 ms delay).

#### User actions and their effects

| Action | Function | Effect |
|---|---|---|
| Accept EA | `acceptEA()` | Sets `overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories`, writes `ea: "accepted"`, closes EA modal. If also `isLowCarb && !stored.carb`, opens carb modal after 350 ms. |
| Decline EA | `declineEA()` | Writes `ea: "declined"`, closes EA modal. Chains to carb modal if needed. |
| Backdrop / Escape (EA) | `closeEAModal()` | Closes modal only — **no decision stored**. Modal will re-appear on next page load. |
| Accept Carb | `acceptCarb()` | Sets `overrideCarbs = carbRecommendedG`. Recalculates calories if carb-based total > current calories. Writes `carb: "accepted"`, closes carb modal. |
| Decline Carb | `declineCarb()` | Writes `carb: "declined"`, closes carb modal. |
| Backdrop / Escape (Carb) | `closeCarbModal()` | Closes modal only — **no decision stored**. |

#### Dashboard wiring

```typescript
const fcOverride = useFightCampOverride({
  userId: user?.id,
  date: selectedDate,
  effectiveTargets,
  isFightCamp: effectiveTargets?.mode === "fight_camp",
  planFingerprint: effectiveTargets
    ? `${effectiveTargets.planId}-${effectiveTargets.planFightDate}-${effectiveTargets.planTargetWeight}`
    : undefined,
});
```

The hook's `overrideCalories` and `overrideCarbs` are applied in the `adjustedTargets` computation:
```typescript
// In dashboard adjustedTargets useMemo:
const calories = fcOverride.overrideCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCalories;
const carbs    = fcOverride.overrideCarbs    ?? effectiveTargets.targetCarbs;
```

---

### 9.10 Low Energy Availability (EA) modal

**Source:** `dashboard.tsx` lines ~1830–1878
**Trigger:** `fcOverride.eaModalOpen === true`
**data-testid:** `dialog-ea-warning`

```
DialogTitle: "Low energy availability"
DialogDesc:  "Your current intake appears to be below the level typically used to support
              recovery and performance (<30 kcal/kg FFM).

              Increasing your intake may help improve energy levels, training quality, and
              recovery. This may slightly slow the rate of weight loss, but can better
              support performance during training.

              This is general performance guidance, not medical advice."

Info row 1:  "Current EA"                → {eaValue} kcal/kg FFM
                                            {targetCalories} kcal/day (sub-label)

[Adjust target to {eaRecommendedCalories} kcal]   data-testid="button-ea-accept"
```

### 9.11 Low Carbohydrate modal

**Source:** `dashboard.tsx` lines ~1880–1927
**Trigger:** `fcOverride.carbModalOpen === true`
**data-testid:** `dialog-carb-warning`

```
DialogTitle: "Low carbohydrate intake"
DialogDesc:  "Carbohydrate intake is below the minimum recommended for athletes
              (~3 g/kg bodyweight). This may impact training performance and recovery
              (IOC / ISSN guidelines)."

Info row 1:  "Current carbs"    → {carbsPerKg} g/kg
Info row 2:  "Suggested minimum" → {carbRecommendedG} g (3 g/kg) (text-primary)

[Adjust carbs to {carbRecommendedG}g]   data-testid="button-carb-accept"
[Keep current plan]                      data-testid="button-carb-decline"  (variant=outline)
```

`onOpenChange`: backdrop/Escape calls `fcOverride.closeCarbModal()` — does NOT record a decision.

**Note on calorie recalculation on accept:** `acceptCarb()` checks if the carb-based calorie total (`protein×4 + fat×9 + carbs×4`) exceeds the current calories (post any EA override). If it does, `overrideCalories` is raised to match, preventing an impossible macro split.

### 9.12 Fight Camp Notification Overlay (fcModal)

**Source:** `WeightCutHero.tsx`, rendered via `createPortal(…, document.body)`
**Purpose:** Full-screen celebration / weight trend notification. Separate from the EA/carb consent modals above — this is a non-blocking notice.

#### Trigger events

| User action / event | Title | `isUp` |
|---|---|---|
| New weight logged, weight ↑ vs prior day | "Weight naturally fluctuates" + body | `true` |
| New weight logged, weight ↓ or flat | "On trend ↓" + body | `false` |
| consistencyCount crosses 3 | "Building rhythm 🔥" | `false` |
| consistencyCount crosses 5 | "Great momentum 🥊" | `false` |
| consistencyCount crosses 6 | "Excellent 💪" | `false` |
| New plan created | "Fight camp set 🎯" + weeks text + chart | `false` |

#### Queue system

The hook uses a modal + queue state pair:
- `setFcModal(data)` — shows immediately if nothing is open
- If one is already open, pushes to `fcModalQueue`
- When `fcModal` goes null (dismissed/timed-out), a `setTimeout(350ms)` dequeues the next item

#### Auto-dismiss

Every modal auto-dismisses after **4500 ms** (`setTimeout(() => dismissFcModal(), 4500)`). The backdrop tap also dismisses immediately.

#### Rendering

Uses `createPortal` to `document.body`. `AnimatePresence` + `motion.div`:

```
Overlay:  fixed inset-0 z-[9999] bg-black/65  (data-testid="fight-camp-notice-overlay")
Card:     mx-6 max-w-sm bg-card rounded-2xl p-7 shadow-2xl
          border: isUp → border-amber-400/25 : border-primary/20
          (data-testid="fight-camp-notice-card")

Inside card:
  Icon: isUp → TrendingUp (amber) : Flame (text-primary/60)
  Title: text-lg font-bold   isUp → text-amber-400 : text-foreground
  Body:  text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2
  [Share this moment] button → opens ShareMomentSheet  (data-testid="button-share-moment")
  "Tap backdrop to dismiss" note
```

Entry animation: `initial={{ opacity:0, scale:0.9, y:16 }}` → `animate={{ opacity:1, scale:1, y:0 }}` (0.26s, 0.06s delay).

#### Share integration

Tapping "Share this moment" in the fcModal:
1. Sets `shareData` from the modal's `{ title, body, emoji, chartType, projectedCut, currentWeight, targetWeight }`
2. Calls `dismissFcModal()`
3. Opens `ShareMomentSheet` (`shareOpen = true`)

The hero card also has a persistent `data-testid="button-demo-share"` button for testing share flow without waiting for a trigger event.

### 9.13 WeightCutPlanner (training page variant)

**Component:** `client/src/components/WeightCutPlanner.tsx`
**Usage:** Embedded on the Training page (not the dashboard). Simpler than `WeightCutHero` — no inline weight logging, no fcModal queue, no share integration, no pace logic.

#### Differences from WeightCutHero

| Feature | WeightCutHero | WeightCutPlanner |
|---|---|---|
| Inline weight logging | ✅ | ❌ |
| fcModal celebration overlay | ✅ | ❌ |
| Share moment | ✅ | ❌ |
| Weigh-in timing toggle in modal | ✅ | ❌ |
| Advanced (manual temp override) | ✅ | ❌ |
| Pace badge + breakdown dialog | ✅ | ❌ |
| Weekly targets collapsible | ❌ | ✅ |
| `fatLossRequired` / `tempCut` | ✅ | ❌ |
| `suggestedDeficitKcal` | ✅ | ✅ |

#### Edit modal (WeightCutPlanner)

Three fields only (no timing, no advanced):
- Current Weight (kg) — `data-testid="input-cut-current-weight"`
- Target Weight (kg) — `data-testid="input-cut-target-weight"`
- Fight Date — `data-testid="input-cut-fight-date"`
- Submit — `data-testid="button-submit-cut-plan"` ("Update Plan" / "Create Plan")

Always uses `POST /api/me/weight-cut` (replace semantics).

#### Summary-only variant (`WeightCutSummaryCard`)

A read-only compact card exported from the same file (`data-testid="card-weight-cut-summary"`):
```
Target icon + "Weight Cut" + Badge "{weeksUntil}w — {weeklyRate} kg/wk"
"{currentWeight} → {targetWeight} kg" + "{daysUntil} days left"
```
Used in places that need a small at-a-glance view without edit controls.
