### 9.14 Energy Availability — Complete End-to-End Reference

> **Scope:** This section documents every part of the EA and carb-floor override feature as it relates to the **Daily Intake Estimates** card on the dashboard. All EA logic is **Fight Camp only** — it does not exist for standard fat-loss, maintenance, or weight-gain goals. Non-fight-camp users never see the EA row, EA modal, or carb modal.

#### 9.14.0 Server vs Client responsibility map

| Responsibility | Location | What it does |
|---|---|---|
| EA formula | 🖥️ **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Computes `ffmKg`, `eaValue`, `isLowEA`, `eaRecommendedCalories` |
| Carb floor formula | 🖥️ **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Computes `carbsPerKg`, `isLowCarb`, `carbRecommendedG` |
| Soft carb performance warning | 🖥️ **SERVER** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` | Sets `isBelowPerformanceCarb` + `performanceCarbWarning` string |
| Override decision storage | 💻 **CLIENT** `useFightCampOverride` hook | Reads/writes `localStorage`, exposes `overrideCalories` / `overrideCarbs` |
| Auto-opening modals | 💻 **CLIENT** `useFightCampOverride` hook | Reacts to `isLowEA` / `isLowCarb` flags from server |
| Final target merging | 💻 **CLIENT** `computeAdjustedTargets()` in `dashboard.tsx` | Applies `overrideCalories` / `overrideCarbs` on top of server values |
| EA row display | 💻 **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Renders inline EA row inside Daily Intake Estimates card |
| EA modal UI | 💻 **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Full-screen Dialog, sourced from `fcOverride.eaModalOpen` |
| Carb modal UI | 💻 **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` JSX | Full-screen Dialog, sourced from `fcOverride.carbModalOpen` |
| Performance toast | 💻 **CLIENT** `dashboard.tsx` `useEffect` | Fires once per date when `isBelowPerformanceCarb` + `shouldShowPerfToast` |

---

#### 9.14.1 🖥️ SERVER — EA and carb-floor calculation

**Route:** `GET /api/me/targets/effective` — fight camp branch only

**Step 1 — Fat-free mass**
```
bodyFatPct = user.bodyFatPct ?? 0.15   ← defaults 15% if not set
ffmKg      = currentWeight × (1 − bodyFatPct)
```

**Step 2 — Energy Availability value**
```
eaValue = (plannedCalories − exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
         ↑ plannedCalories = tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAddedBack − plannedDeficitKcal
         ↑ exerciseKcalAdjusted = sum of all session estimatedKcal (0 on rest day)
```
`eaValue` is the number of kcal available per kg of fat-free mass after exercise is accounted for.

**Step 3 — Hard EA flag**
```
isLowEA = eaValue < 30          ← IOC RED-S threshold
eaRecommendedCalories = Math.round(exerciseKcalAdjusted + 30 × ffmKg)
                        ← minimum calories that exactly hits EA = 30
```

**Step 4 — Hard carb floor flag**
```
carbsPerKg  = targetCarbs / currentWeight
isLowCarb   = exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0 && !isRestDay && carbsPerKg < 3
              ← only fires on actual training days with calories burned
carbRecommendedG = Math.round(3 × currentWeight)   ← IOC/ISSN minimum
```

**Step 5 — Soft performance warning** (only if `!isLowCarb`)
```
if dayType === "hard"      && carbsPerKg < 4 → isBelowPerformanceCarb = true
if dayType === "very_hard" && carbsPerKg < 5 → isBelowPerformanceCarb = true
// moderate / light: hard floor at 3 g/kg already covers them; no separate soft threshold
```
`performanceCarbWarning` string is set with the appropriate message per day type.

**Step 6 — Response fields** (subset relevant to EA/carb feature)
```json
{
  "ffmKg":                 72.3,
  "eaValue":               28.4,
  "isLowEA":               true,
  "isLowCarb":             false,
  "carbsPerKg":            2.6,
  "eaRecommendedCalories": 2344,
  "carbRecommendedG":      219,
  "isBelowPerformanceCarb": false,
  "performanceCarbWarning": null,
  "planId":                7,
  "planFightDate":         "2026-09-15",
  "planTargetWeight":      70.0
}
```
The last three fields (`planId`, `planFightDate`, `planTargetWeight`) are included so the client can build the `planFingerprint` that detects plan changes and re-triggers consent modals.

---

#### 9.14.2 💻 CLIENT — `useFightCampOverride` hook — decision layer

**File:** `client/src/hooks/useFightCampOverride.ts`

This hook is the sole manager of override state. It never calls any API.

##### localStorage key

```
fightCamp:{userId}:{date}:{planId}:{fightDate}:{targetWeight}
```
If the user modifies the fight camp plan (different date, different target weight, new plan), the fingerprint changes → new key → stored decisions are not found → modals auto-trigger again for the new plan.

##### Stored value shape
```typescript
{
  ea?: "accepted" | "declined",
  carb?: "accepted" | "declined",
  perfToastShown?: boolean
}
```

##### Decision restoration on load

When `storageKey`, `date`, or `effectiveTargets` changes (including initial page load):
```typescript
// If ea === "accepted" and server still reports eaRecommendedCalories:
setOverrideCalories(effectiveTargets.eaRecommendedCalories);

// If ea === "declined" (or no decision):
setOverrideCalories(null);   // server value used as-is

// Same pattern for carb:
setOverrideCarbs(carbRecommendedG)   // if accepted
setOverrideCarbs(null)               // if declined / no decision
```

##### Auto-open sequence

Triggered by a `useEffect` watching `isFightCamp`, `isLowEA`, `isLowCarb`, `storageKey`:

```
1. If isLowEA && !stored.ea  → open EA modal immediately
2. Else if isLowCarb && !stored.carb → open carb modal immediately
```
Only one modal is ever open at a time. The carb modal chains via a 350 ms `setTimeout` after either `acceptEA()` or `declineEA()`.

##### Action outcomes

| User action | Function | `overrideCalories` | `overrideCarbs` | Stored | Carb chain? |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Accept EA | `acceptEA()` | `= eaRecommendedCalories` | unchanged | `ea: "accepted"` | Yes, if `isLowCarb && !stored.carb` |
| Decline EA | `declineEA()` | unchanged (`null`) | unchanged | `ea: "declined"` | Yes, if `isLowCarb && !stored.carb` |
| Backdrop / Esc (EA) | `closeEAModal()` | unchanged | unchanged | **nothing written** | No |
| Accept Carb | `acceptCarb()` | bumped up if needed¹ | `= carbRecommendedG` | `carb: "accepted"` | — |
| Decline Carb | `declineCarb()` | unchanged | unchanged (`null`) | `carb: "declined"` | — |
| Backdrop / Esc (Carb) | `closeCarbModal()` | unchanged | unchanged | **nothing written** | — |

¹ `acceptCarb()` bump logic: `carbBasedCals = protein×4 + fat×9 + carbs×4`. If `carbBasedCals > (overrideCalories ?? serverCalories)` → `setOverrideCalories(carbBasedCals)`. This prevents an impossible macro split where carbs alone exceed the calorie target.

**Key rule:** Backdrop/Escape never records a decision. The modal re-appears every time the page loads until the user explicitly taps Accept or Keep Plan.

---

#### 9.14.3 💻 CLIENT — `computeAdjustedTargets()` — merging overrides

In `dashboard.tsx`, `computeAdjustedTargets()` is called each render (no memo) and produces `adjustedTargets`, which drives every number displayed in the Daily Intake Estimates card.

```typescript
// Fight camp branch only:
const finalCals = fcOverride.overrideCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCalories;

let finalCarbs:
  if (fcOverride.overrideCarbs != null)         → fcOverride.overrideCarbs
  else if (fcOverride.overrideCalories != null) → Math.round(
                                                    Math.max(0,
                                                      overrideCalories
                                                      − serverProtein×4
                                                      − serverFat×9
                                                    ) / 4
                                                  )   // extra cals go to carbs
  else                                          → effectiveTargets.targetCarbs

// Re-computed effective EA from final values (for display):
effectiveEA = (finalCals − exerciseKcal) / ffmKg

// Re-computed flags (after any override):
isLowEA  = effectiveEA < 30
isLowCarb = (finalCarbs / bodyWeightKg) < 3 && exerciseKcal > 0

// Preserved server originals — remain true even after override brings EA to 30:
originallyLowEA   = effectiveTargets.isLowEA   // drives "adjusted ✓" indicator
originallyLowCarb = effectiveTargets.isLowCarb
```

> ⚠️ The client **re-computes** `isLowEA` and `isLowCarb` after applying overrides. This means: once the user accepts the EA fix and `overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories`, `isLowEA` becomes `false` (EA is now exactly 30), but `originallyLowEA` stays `true` so the "adjusted ✓" state can still be shown.

---

#### 9.14.4 💻 CLIENT — EA row inside the Daily Intake Estimates card

This inline row appears **only in fight camp mode** and only when `adjustedTargets.eaValue != null`.

##### Normal / OK state (isLowEA = false)
```
div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-xs
               bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"
```

##### Warning state (isLowEA = true AND eaDecision ≠ "accepted")
```
div className="… bg-orange-500/10 border border-orange-500/30 text-orange-400"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openEAModal}
          className="text-[10px] underline underline-offset-2 opacity-80 hover:opacity-100"
          data-testid="button-ea-review">
    {eaDecision === "declined" ? "Review" : "Review →"}
  </button>
```
Label changes from "Review →" to plain "Review" after the user has explicitly declined (so they know it was already considered).

##### Accepted state (originallyLowEA = true AND eaDecision = "accepted")
```
div className="… bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-ea-value"

  "Energy Availability"
  "{eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"   ← now ≥ 30 after override
  "· adjusted ✓"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openEAModal}
          data-testid="button-ea-review-accepted">
    Review
  </button>
```

##### Low carb inline warning (isLowCarb = true AND carbDecision ≠ "accepted")
```
div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-xs
               bg-yellow-500/10 border border-yellow-500/30 text-yellow-400"
  data-testid="text-low-carb-warning"

  "Carbs below 3 g/kg"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openCarbModal}
          data-testid="button-carb-review">
    {carbDecision === "declined" ? "Review" : "Review →"}
  </button>
```

##### Low carb accepted state (originallyLowCarb = true AND carbDecision = "accepted")
```
div className="… bg-secondary/50 text-muted-foreground"
  data-testid="text-carb-adjusted"

  "Carbs adjusted to 3 g/kg"
  "· adjusted ✓"
  <button onClick={fcOverride.openCarbModal}
          data-testid="button-carb-review-accepted">
    Review
  </button>
```

---

#### 9.14.5 💻 CLIENT — EA modal (full specification)

**Trigger:** `fcOverride.eaModalOpen === true`  
**Container:** `sm:max-w-sm`  `data-testid="dialog-ea-warning"`  
**`onOpenChange`:** backdrop/Escape → `fcOverride.closeEAModal()` — **no decision stored**

```
DialogTitle:  "Low energy availability"

DialogDesc:   "Your current intake appears to be below the level typically used to
               support recovery and performance (<30 kcal/kg FFM).

               Increasing your intake may help improve energy levels, training
               quality, and recovery. This may slightly slow the rate of weight
               loss, but can better support performance during training.

               This is general performance guidance, not medical advice."

─── Info rows (space-y-3 py-2) ──────────────────────────────────────────────

Row 1:
  Left:  "Current EA"             (text-muted-foreground)
  Right: "{effectiveTargets.eaValue} kcal/kg FFM"   (font-semibold tabular-nums)
         "{effectiveTargets.targetCalories} kcal/day"  (sub-label: text-xs font-normal text-muted-foreground)

Row 2:
  Left:  "Calories needed for EA 30"  (text-muted-foreground)
  Right: "{eaRecommendedCalories} kcal"   (font-semibold tabular-nums text-primary)

─── Buttons (flex-col gap-2 pt-1) ───────────────────────────────────────────

[Adjust target to {eaRecommendedCalories} kcal]
  className="w-full"
  data-testid="button-ea-accept"
  onClick → fcOverride.acceptEA()
    ↳ setOverrideCalories(eaRecommendedCalories)
    ↳ writeStorage({ ea: "accepted" })
    ↳ closes EA modal
    ↳ if isLowCarb && !stored.carb: opens carb modal after 350 ms

[Keep current plan]
  variant="outline"  className="w-full"
  data-testid="button-ea-decline"
  onClick → fcOverride.declineEA()
    ↳ writeStorage({ ea: "declined" })
    ↳ closes EA modal
    ↳ if isLowCarb && !stored.carb: opens carb modal after 350 ms
```

---

#### 9.14.6 💻 CLIENT — Carb modal (full specification)

**Trigger:** `fcOverride.carbModalOpen === true`  
**Container:** `sm:max-w-sm`  `data-testid="dialog-carb-warning"`  
**`onOpenChange`:** backdrop/Escape → `fcOverride.closeCarbModal()` — **no decision stored**

```
DialogTitle:  "Low carbohydrate intake"

DialogDesc:   "Carbohydrate intake is below the minimum recommended for athletes
               (~3 g/kg bodyweight). This may impact training performance and
               recovery (IOC / ISSN guidelines)."

─── Info rows (space-y-3 py-2) ──────────────────────────────────────────────

Row 1:
  Left:  "Current carbs"     (text-muted-foreground)
  Right: "{effectiveTargets.carbsPerKg} g/kg"   (font-semibold tabular-nums)

Row 2:
  Left:  "Suggested minimum"  (text-muted-foreground)
  Right: "{carbRecommendedG} g (3 g/kg)"   (font-semibold tabular-nums text-primary)

─── Buttons (flex-col gap-2 pt-1) ───────────────────────────────────────────

[Adjust carbs to {carbRecommendedG}g]
  className="w-full"
  data-testid="button-carb-accept"
  onClick → fcOverride.acceptCarb()
    ↳ setOverrideCarbs(carbRecommendedG)
    ↳ carbBasedCals = protein×4 + fat×9 + carbRecommendedG×4
    ↳ if carbBasedCals > currentCalories: setOverrideCalories(carbBasedCals)
    ↳ writeStorage({ carb: "accepted" })
    ↳ closes carb modal

[Keep current plan]
  variant="outline"  className="w-full"
  data-testid="button-carb-decline"
  onClick → fcOverride.declineCarb()
    ↳ writeStorage({ carb: "declined" })
    ↳ closes carb modal
```

---

#### 9.14.7 💻 CLIENT — Soft performance toast

This is a non-blocking advisory — no modal, no user action required.

**Trigger conditions (all must be true):**
1. `effectiveTargets.mode === "fight_camp"`
2. `effectiveTargets.isBelowPerformanceCarb === true`
3. `effectiveTargets.performanceCarbWarning` is a non-empty string
4. `fcOverride.shouldShowPerfToast === true` (i.e. `perfToastShown` not yet in storage for this key)

**Timing:** 1500 ms `setTimeout` after the `useEffect` fires (delayed to avoid clashing with page load).

```typescript
toast({
  title: "Performance note",
  description: effectiveTargets.performanceCarbWarning,
});
fcOverride.markPerfToastShown();
// writes { perfToastShown: true } to localStorage — toast never repeats for this plan/date
```

**Server-side warning strings by day type:**

| Day type | Carbs threshold | `performanceCarbWarning` |
|---|---|---|
| `hard` | < 4 g/kg | "Carbohydrate intake may be low for this training load. Increasing toward ~5 g/kg may support performance." |
| `very_hard` | < 5 g/kg | "Carbohydrate intake may be low for a very high training load. Increasing toward ~5–7 g/kg may support performance." |
| `moderate` / `light` | covered by hard carb modal | *(not set — hard modal fires at < 3 g/kg)* |

---

#### 9.14.8 Complete decision flow diagram

```
Page loads / date changes
       │
       ▼
GET /api/me/targets/effective  ← 🖥️ SERVER
  computes: eaValue, isLowEA, isLowCarb,
            eaRecommendedCalories, carbRecommendedG,
            isBelowPerformanceCarb, performanceCarbWarning
       │
       ▼
useFightCampOverride() reads localStorage     ← 💻 CLIENT
  ├─ ea === "accepted"   → restore overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories
  ├─ ea === "declined"   → overrideCalories = null (server value used)
  └─ ea === undefined    → check isLowEA…
       │
       ├─ isLowEA && !stored.ea
       │    └─ OPEN EA MODAL
       │         ├─ [Adjust] acceptEA()
       │         │    overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories ──────────┐
       │         │    stored: { ea: "accepted" }                         │
       │         │    → chain carb modal if needed (350 ms)              │
       │         ├─ [Keep plan] declineEA()                              │
       │         │    overrideCalories = null                             │
       │         │    stored: { ea: "declined" }                         │
       │         │    → chain carb modal if needed (350 ms)              │
       │         └─ [Backdrop/Esc] closeEAModal()                        │
       │              nothing stored — modal re-appears next load         │
       │                                                                  │
       └─ isLowCarb && !stored.carb                                      │
            └─ OPEN CARB MODAL (or chained from EA modal)               │
                 ├─ [Adjust] acceptCarb()                                │
                 │    overrideCarbs = carbRecommendedG                   │
                 │    if carbCals > currentCals: overrideCalories ↑ ←───┘
                 │    stored: { carb: "accepted" }
                 ├─ [Keep plan] declineCarb()
                 │    overrideCarbs = null
                 │    stored: { carb: "declined" }
                 └─ [Backdrop/Esc] closeCarbModal()
                      nothing stored — modal re-appears next load

computeAdjustedTargets()   ← 💻 CLIENT
  finalCals  = overrideCalories ?? serverCalories
  finalCarbs = overrideCarbs ?? (overrideCalories → recalculate) ?? serverCarbs
  effectiveEA re-computed from finalCals

Daily Intake Estimates card renders:   ← 💻 CLIENT
  ┌─ EA row: normal / warning / accepted
  ├─ Carb row: warning / accepted (if applicable)
  └─ Macro grid: finalCals / serverProtein / finalCarbs / serverFat

Performance toast (separate path):   ← 💻 CLIENT
  isBelowPerformanceCarb && shouldShowPerfToast
    → toast after 1500 ms → perfToastShown persisted
```

---

#### 9.14.9 All data-testids for the EA feature

| Element | data-testid |
|---|---|
| EA row in card (all states) | `text-ea-value` |
| "Review →" button (low EA, not yet accepted) | `button-ea-review` |
| "Review" button (EA already accepted) | `button-ea-review-accepted` |
| Low carb inline warning row | `text-low-carb-warning` |
| "Review →" button (low carb, not yet accepted) | `button-carb-review` |
| Low carb accepted row | `text-carb-adjusted` |
| "Review" button (carb already accepted) | `button-carb-review-accepted` |
| EA modal | `dialog-ea-warning` |
| EA modal "Adjust target" button | `button-ea-accept` |
| EA modal "Keep current plan" button | `button-ea-decline` |
| Carb modal | `dialog-carb-warning` |
| Carb modal "Adjust carbs" button | `button-carb-accept` |
| Carb modal "Keep current plan" button | `button-carb-decline` |

---

#### 9.14.10 Edge cases and important rules

| Rule | Detail |
|---|---|
| EA floor is advisory, not enforced | Server does NOT clamp `targetCalories` to `eaRecommendedCalories`. It passes both values and lets the user decide. |
| Carb floor is advisory only | `isLowCarb` is a flag — the server does not bump `targetCarbs` to 3 g/kg automatically. |
| Rest days exempt from both floors | `isLowEA` can still fire (no training = lower denominator), but `isLowCarb` will not (`exerciseKcalAdjusted === 0` required for carb floor). |
| EA modal takes priority | Auto-open checks EA first, carb second. Carb modal is always chained after EA is resolved (350 ms delay), never opened simultaneously. |
| Plan change clears all decisions | If `planId`, `planFightDate`, or `planTargetWeight` change, the storage key changes and no prior decisions are found → all modals re-trigger. |
| Backdrop never persists | Dismissing either modal via backdrop or Escape writes nothing to storage. Only explicit button clicks (`acceptEA`, `declineEA`, `acceptCarb`, `declineCarb`) are persisted. |
| `originallyLow*` is from server | After accepting the EA override, the client's re-computed `isLowEA` becomes `false`. The `originallyLowEA` field keeps the server's original `true` so the "adjusted ✓" badge can still appear. |
| Body fat default | If `user.bodyFatPct` is null, the server assumes 15% BF for FFM calculation. Users can update body fat % in their profile to improve accuracy. |

---

### 9.15 Training → Target Reconciliation

> **Why this section exists:** Adding, editing, or deleting a training session changes how many calories the user burned. Both the calorie target shown in the Daily Intake Estimates card **and** the EA/carb floor checks must update immediately to reflect that change. This section documents the full end-to-end chain — from the training mutation to the updated card numbers and (if needed) the re-opened consent modals.

---

#### 9.15.0 The two add-back models

There are two completely different paths depending on whether Fight Camp mode is active. Mobile replicators must implement both separately.

| | Fight Camp mode | Standard goals (fat loss / maintenance / weight gain) |
|---|---|---|
| **Who adds training calories** | 🖥️ **Server** bakes them into `targetCalories` | 💻 **Client** adds `trainingSummary.totalKcal × creditPct` on top of server base |
| **Client rule** | Use `effectiveTargets.targetCalories` as-is. Do NOT add training again. | Compute `adjustedCalories = baseCalories + round(totalKcal × creditPct)` |
| **Credit percentages** | `trainingCalorieCreditPct: 0` (always returned by server as `0` as a guard) | fat_loss: 50%, maintenance: 75%, weight_gain: 100% |
| **EA / carb checks** | Server computes `isLowEA`, `isLowCarb` and client shows modals | No EA / carb checks — these fields are `false` / `undefined` for non-fight-camp |
| **Macro adjustment** | Protein + fat fixed; carbs absorb remaining calories (server computes) | Protein + fat from profile; extra carbs absorb training credit (client computes) |

---

#### 9.15.1 🖥️ SERVER — how training is read at request time

`GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD` is **not a cached snapshot** — it queries the database live every time it is called.

In the fight camp branch:
```
todaySessions  = storage.getWorkoutSessions(userId, date, date)
todayActivities = flatten(storage.getSessionActivities(session.id) for each session)

exerciseKcalRaw      = sum(session.estimatedKcal for all todaySessions)
                       = 0 when isRestDay
exerciseKcalAdjusted = exerciseKcalRaw          // RPE already baked into estimatedKcal at write time
exerciseKcalAddedBack = round(exerciseKcalAdjusted × 0.8)   // 80% policy

plannedCalories = round(tdeeNoExercise + exerciseKcalAddedBack − plannedDeficitKcal)
targetCalories  = plannedCalories    // EA floor check is advisory only — no clamping

eaValue  = (plannedCalories − exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
isLowEA  = eaValue < 30
isLowCarb = exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0 && !isRestDay && carbsPerKg < 3
```

**Consequence:** If the user goes from 0 sessions to 1 session, `exerciseKcalAdjusted` jumps from 0 to the session's `estimatedKcal`. The next call to `GET /api/me/targets/effective` will return a higher `targetCalories` and potentially new `isLowEA` / `isLowCarb` flags.

---

#### 9.15.2 💻 CLIENT — `estimatedKcal` is baked in at write time

The server bakes RPE into `estimatedKcal` when a session or activity is **created or updated** — not when targets are fetched. The effective-targets route simply sums the stored `estimatedKcal` values.

```
POST /api/workouts/sessions          → creates session, estimatedKcal starts at 0
POST /api/workouts/sessions/:id/exercises → creates exercise, triggers recalculateSessionCalories()
PATCH /api/workouts/exercises/:id    → if rpe/duration changes → re-runs RPE × rawKcal
PATCH /api/workouts/sessions/:id     → if rpe/duration changes on session level → recalculates

POST /api/me/training/manual-burn    → creates a session with estimatedKcal = caloriesBurned directly
```

`recalculateSessionCalories()` (server-side helper):
- Sums `estimatedKcal` across all exercises in the session
- Applies RPE factor: `rpeFactor = 0.85 + (sessionRpe − 1) × 0.05` (RPE 1→0.85, RPE 10→1.30)
- Writes result back to `session.estimatedKcal`
- The target-fetch route reads this stored value — no runtime RPE calculation

---

#### 9.15.3 💻 CLIENT — cache invalidation chain

Every mutation that changes today's training **removes** the cached effective-targets response so the next access triggers a fresh fetch.

| Mutation | Queries removed / invalidated |
|---|---|
| Create session (`POST /api/workouts/sessions`) | `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` |
| Delete session (`DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id`) | same triple |
| Add exercise to session | `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training-load"]` |
| Update exercise (rpe/sets/duration) | same as add exercise |
| Delete exercise | same as add exercise |
| Add/edit/delete activity (cardio) | same as add exercise |
| Mark rest day | `removeQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `removeQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| Manual burn (`POST /api/me/training/manual-burn`) | `invalidateQueries ["/api/workouts/sessions"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| AI log — training intent | `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |
| Morning check-in — session created | `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/training/summary"]` + `invalidateQueries ["/api/me/targets/effective"]` |

**`removeQueries` vs `invalidateQueries`:** `removeQueries` drops the cached data entirely so the next subscriber immediately triggers a network fetch (no stale data shown). `invalidateQueries` marks as stale and re-fetches in the background. Both result in the same eventual state. Training mutations use `removeQueries` on `targets/effective` to guarantee the old number is never shown after training changes.

---

#### 9.15.4 💻 CLIENT — the automatic re-fetch chain

```
Training mutation fires
  │
  └─ onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"], exact: false)
                removeQueries(["/api/me/training/summary"],  exact: false)
       │
       ▼
TanStack Query sees the cache is empty for the active queryKey
       │
       ▼
Re-fetches GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD   ← 🖥️ SERVER
  ↳ reads updated todaySessions from DB
  ↳ returns new targetCalories, eaValue, isLowEA, isLowCarb, etc.
       │
       ▼
React re-renders:
  effectiveTargets updates → computeAdjustedTargets() re-runs
       │
       ├─ Daily Intake Estimates card shows new numbers
       │
       └─ useFightCampOverride useEffect fires (watches isLowEA, isLowCarb, storageKey)
              │
              ├─ if isLowEA && !stored.ea  → open EA modal
              └─ else if isLowCarb && !stored.carb → open carb modal
```

**Key point:** The modal auto-open logic in `useFightCampOverride` runs every time `isLowEA` or `isLowCarb` changes. So if a training session is added that pushes EA below 30, the EA modal **automatically opens** without any extra code — the re-fetch is the only trigger needed.

---

#### 9.15.5 💻 CLIENT — standard goal add-back (non-fight-camp)

For fat loss / maintenance / weight gain, the server returns a flat base target. The client applies the credit:

```typescript
// GET /api/me/training/summary/:date → { totalKcal, totalKcalAdjusted }
// totalKcalAdjusted mirrors totalKcal (RPE baked in at write time)
const trainingKcal = trainingSummary?.totalKcalAdjusted ?? trainingSummary?.totalKcal ?? 0;

const creditPct: Record<string, number> = {
  fat_loss:    0.5,   // 50%
  maintenance: 0.75,  // 75%
  weight_gain: 1.0,   // 100%
};

// From server (base, before training):
const baseCalories = effectiveTargets?.targetCalories ?? user.targetCalories;
const baseCarbs    = effectiveTargets?.targetCarbs    ?? user.targetCarbs;

// Client adds back:
let adjustedCalories = baseCalories + Math.round(trainingKcal * creditPct[goal]);

// Fat-loss cap: deficit ≤ 1% BW/week
if (goal === "fat_loss") {
  const maxDailyDeficit = Math.round((0.01 * bodyWeightKg * 7700) / 7);
  const tdee = effectiveTargets?.tdee ?? baseCalories + 500;
  if (tdee - adjustedCalories > maxDailyDeficit) {
    adjustedCalories = tdee - maxDailyDeficit;
  }
}

// Protein + fat stay fixed; extra calories go to carbs:
const adjustedCarbs = baseCarbs + Math.round(Math.max(0, adjustedCalories - baseCalories) / 4);
```

The standard path **never checks EA or carb floors** — `isLowEA` and `isLowCarb` are always `false`, and no EA/carb modals ever appear.

---

#### 9.15.6 🖥️ SERVER — training summary endpoint

Used by the client (both fight camp and standard) to display session cards and provide `totalKcal` for the non-fight-camp add-back.

```
GET /api/me/training/summary/:date
```

Response:
```json
{
  "date": "2026-06-22",
  "totalKcal": 480,
  "totalKcalAdjusted": 480,
  "isRestDay": false,
  "sessions": [
    { "id": 12, "timeOfDay": "morning", "estimatedKcal": 480,
      "exerciseCount": 4, "activityCount": 1 }
  ]
}
```

`totalKcalAdjusted` mirrors `totalKcal` — RPE is already baked into each session's `estimatedKcal` at storage time, so no further adjustment is needed here.

---

#### 9.15.7 End-to-end example: user adds a 500 kcal session in fight camp

```
Initial state (no training logged today):
  effectiveTargets.targetCalories = 1800   (NEAT + 0 exercise − deficit)
  effectiveTargets.eaValue = 24.6          (LOW — only resting NEAT available)
  effectiveTargets.isLowEA = true
  → EA modal opens on page load

User dismisses modal (backdrop tap) — no decision stored

User navigates to Training page → creates a morning session
  POST /api/workouts/sessions { date, timeOfDay: "morning" }
  onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"])

TanStack Query re-fetches GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=2026-06-22
  Server reads session: estimatedKcal = 0 (no exercises yet)
  exerciseKcalAdjusted = 0 → targetCalories still 1800, isLowEA still true

User adds a 60-min run activity (MET 9.5, 75 kg → ~285 kcal) with RPE 7
  POST /api/workouts/sessions/:id/activities  { durationMinutes:60, metValue:9.5, rpe:7 }
  Server: rawKcal = 9.5×3.5×75/200×60 = 748 → wait, estimatedKcal = 285 (MET formula)
          rpeFactor = 0.85 + (7−1)×0.05 = 1.15
          estimatedKcal = round(285 × 1.15) = 328
  recalculateSessionCalories() writes session.estimatedKcal = 328
  onSuccess: removeQueries(["/api/me/targets/effective"])

TanStack Query re-fetches targets:
  exerciseKcalAdjusted = 328
  exerciseKcalAddedBack = round(328 × 0.8) = 262
  plannedCalories = 1800_base + 262 = 2062  (using tdeeNoExercise, not the old 1800)
  ffmKg = 63.75 (75 kg × 0.85)
  eaValue = (2062 − 328) / 63.75 = 27.2    (still < 30)
  isLowEA = true → EA modal re-opens (no stored decision yet)
  isLowCarb = 328 > 0 && carbsPerKg < 3 → possibly true

User accepts EA modal:
  overrideCalories = eaRecommendedCalories = round(328 + 30 × 63.75) = 2241
  stored: { ea: "accepted" }
  → carb modal chains if isLowCarb

Card now shows:
  Calories: 2241
  EA row: "27.2 → 30.0 kcal/kg FFM · adjusted ✓"
```

---

#### 9.15.8 What a mobile app must implement

If you are building a mobile app and currently not reconciling training with targets, here is the minimum required implementation:

**Step 1 — After any training mutation, re-fetch effective targets**
```
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id/exercises
POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/workouts/sessions/:id/activities
POST /api/me/training/manual-burn
POST/DELETE /api/me/rest-day/:date
  → onSuccess: invalidate / re-fetch GET /api/me/targets/effective?date=YYYY-MM-DD
                                      GET /api/me/training/summary/:date
```

**Step 2 — Use the right calorie source**

| Mode | Calorie target to display |
|---|---|
| Fight camp (`effectiveTargets.mode === "fight_camp"`) | `effectiveTargets.targetCalories` directly (already includes training) |
| Standard goals | `effectiveTargets.targetCalories + round(trainingSummary.totalKcal × creditPct)` |

**Step 3 — Check EA / carb flags after each re-fetch (fight camp only)**

After re-fetching `effectiveTargets`:
```
if mode === "fight_camp":
  if isLowEA && no stored ea decision for this date/plan:
    → show EA consent modal

  elif isLowCarb && no stored carb decision for this date/plan:
    → show carb consent modal

  if isBelowPerformanceCarb && soft toast not yet shown:
    → show advisory toast after 1500 ms
```

**Step 4 — Apply user overrides on top of server values**
```
displayCalories = overrideCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCalories
displayCarbs    = overrideCarbs    ?? recalculatedFromDisplayCalories ?? effectiveTargets.targetCarbs
```

**What NOT to do:**
- ❌ Don't add `trainingSummary.totalKcal` to `targetCalories` in fight camp — it's already included
- ❌ Don't cache `targetCalories` at app startup and use it for the day — it changes as training is logged
- ❌ Don't skip the re-fetch after deleting a session — removing training lowers the target and may change EA flags
- ❌ Don't re-trigger EA modals if the user already accepted/declined for this plan+date (check localStorage / your local decision store first)

---

### 9.16 isLowEA / isLowCarb — Warning Flag Reference

This section documents the exact conditions under which the two nutritional-warning flags are set, the server/client split of responsibility, and the design decisions behind each rule. Both flags appear in the `GET /api/me/targets/effective` response and drive the warning rows inside the **Daily Intake Estimates** card.

---

#### 9.16.0 Where each flag lives

| Flag | Server field | Client field | Who computes final value |
|---|---|---|---|
| `isLowEA` | `effectiveTargets.isLowEA` | Re-read from server response | **Server only** — client always trusts it |
| `isLowCarb` | `effectiveTargets.isLowCarb` | `isLowCarbFinal` (see §9.16.3) | Server for standard mode; client overrides **only** in Fight Camp when `overrideCarbs != null` |

---

#### 9.16.1 isLowEA — Energy Availability warning

**Server code location:** `server/routes.ts` → `GET /api/me/targets/effective`

**Condition (all must be true):**

```
isLowEA = true   when:
  fightCampActive === true
  AND energyAvailability < 30          // kcal / kg FFM
```

Where:
```
energyAvailability = (calorieTarget - exerciseKcalAdjusted) / ffmKg
```

`ffmKg` is derived from user body fat if available, otherwise estimated from a lean-population formula.

**Threshold: 30 kcal/kg FFM**  
This is the internationally recognised RED-S / LEA threshold for combat athletes. Below this, the user is at clinical risk of Relative Energy Deficiency in Sport.

**No `hasActualActivities` guard on isLowEA** — even with zero exercise today, a fight-camp calorie target that is structurally low relative to FFM should still warn.

**UI trigger:** Low-EA row in Daily Intake Estimates card → "Review →" opens EA warning Dialog (§9.10).

---

#### 9.16.2 isLowCarb — Low-carbohydrate warning (server side)

**Server code location:** `server/routes.ts` → `GET /api/me/targets/effective`

**Condition (all must be true):**

```typescript
const hasActualActivities = todayActivities.length > 0;

isLowCarb = true   when:
  hasActualActivities === true          // at least one logged activity today
  AND exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0          // that training burns real calories
  AND isRestDay === false               // user has not marked the day as rest
  AND carbsPerKg < 3                    // g carbs / kg bodyweight below performance threshold
```

`carbsPerKg = targetCarbs / weightKg`  
`targetCarbs` is the server-computed carbohydrate target for the day (fight-camp or standard).

**Why `hasActualActivities` exists:**  
Without this guard, a rest day or a day where the user has not logged any training yet would generate a false-positive low-carb warning purely because the baseline macro targets happen to set carbs below 3 g/kg. The warning is only meaningful when real training load has been confirmed.

**`isBelowPerformanceCarb`** (separate flag, same file) uses the same `hasActualActivities` guard and a lower threshold (< 2 g/kg) to drive the more urgent "performance carb" state.

**UI trigger:** Low-carb warning row in Daily Intake Estimates card → "Review →" opens Carb warning Dialog (§9.11).

---

#### 9.16.3 isLowCarb — Client-side resolution (`computeAdjustedTargets`)

**Client code location:** `client/src/pages/dashboard.tsx` → `computeAdjustedTargets()`

The client must resolve a final `isLowCarbFinal` value for rendering. The rule is:

```typescript
// fcOverride = result of useFightCampOverride()
const isLowCarbFinal =
  fcOverride.overrideCarbs != null
    ? effectiveCarbsPerKg < 3          // FC active + carb override present → recompute locally
    : (effectiveTargets?.isLowCarb ?? false);  // all other cases → trust server
```

**When `overrideCarbs != null` (Fight Camp active, carb override applied):**  
The fight-camp hook may adjust carbs beyond what the server already computed. The client recomputes `effectiveCarbsPerKg` from the final adjusted carb target, then applies the same `< 3` threshold. This avoids a stale server value when the carb override shifts the target mid-session.

**All other cases:**  
The client reads `effectiveTargets.isLowCarb` directly from the server. The client does **not** re-evaluate the `hasActualActivities` guard — it trusts the server's result unconditionally.

> ⚠️ **Do not** replicate the full `isLowCarb` logic on the client for non-FC cases. The server has access to `todayActivities` (the actual logged sessions array) which is not separately available on the client. Re-computing it from macro targets alone would reproduce the false-positive bug that was fixed by the `hasActualActivities` guard.

---

#### 9.16.4 Complete conditions table

| Scenario | `hasActualActivities` | `isRestDay` | `exerciseKcalAdjusted` | `carbsPerKg` | `isLowCarb` (server) |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Rest day (marked) | any | **true** | any | any | **false** |
| No sessions logged yet | **false** | false | any | any | **false** |
| Session logged, carbs ≥ 3 g/kg | true | false | > 0 | ≥ 3 | **false** |
| Session logged, carbs < 3 g/kg | true | false | > 0 | < 3 | **true** |
| Session logged, 0 kcal burn | true | false | **0** | < 3 | **false** |

---

#### 9.16.5 Key design decisions

1. **Server is source of truth for `isLowEA` always.** Energy availability requires `ffmKg`, which involves body-fat estimation logic that lives only on the server.

2. **Server is source of truth for `isLowCarb` in standard mode.** `todayActivities` (the raw session list for the day) is fetched inside the `/targets/effective` handler and is not separately exposed on a client-readable endpoint that would be available at render time.

3. **Client overrides `isLowCarb` only in Fight Camp + carb-override active.** This is the single case where the fight-camp hook adjusts carbs beyond what the server target already shows, and the server's cached flag would be stale.

4. **`hasActualActivities` uses `todayActivities.length > 0`, not a calorie threshold.** A session can be logged with 0 kcal estimated burn (e.g. yoga, mobility). The double-guard (`hasActualActivities && exerciseKcalAdjusted > 0`) ensures both that a session exists AND that it actually contributes load.

5. **`isRestDay` gates both `isLowCarb` and `isBelowPerformanceCarb`.** Rest days are expected to have lower carb targets; warning on them would be noise.

6. **The 3 g/kg threshold is sport-science consensus** for minimum carbohydrate availability during moderate-to-high training volume for combat athletes. 2 g/kg (`isBelowPerformanceCarb`) is the acute-performance-impairment floor.

7. **No debounce on the warning.** If training is deleted, the next `/targets/effective` fetch will drop `isLowCarb` back to `false`. The cache invalidation chain in §9.15.3 ensures this re-fetch happens automatically after session changes.

8. **Modal re-trigger prevention** (EA modal only, §9.10) is managed client-side via `localStorage`. The key is `ea_modal_dismissed_{userId}_{planId}_{date}`. isLowCarb has no equivalent suppression — the carb warning row is always shown when the flag is true.

---


### 10.1 Calorie burn estimation
Defined in `server/lib/energy.ts`.

#### Core MET formula (`kcalFromMET`)
```
kcal/min = MET × 3.5 × bodyWeightKg / 200
sessionKcal = kcal/min × durationMinutes
```
Returns 0 if any input is zero or negative.

#### Strength training METs (`getStrengthMET`)
Used when no MET value comes from the activity catalog:
```
light    → 3.5
moderate → 5.0  ← default when intensity is null/unknown
vigorous → 6.0
```

#### Session calorie calculator (`calculateSessionCalories`)
```typescript
calculateSessionCalories(
  weightKg: number,
  input: {
    durationMinutes?: number | null,
    intensity?: string | null,
    sets?: Array<{ restSeconds?: number | null }>,
    activities?: Array<{ metValue: number; durationMinutes: number }>
  }
): { totalKcal, strengthKcal, activityKcal, estimatedMinutes }
```
- If `durationMinutes` is not provided but `sets` are, duration is **estimated from sets** (see below)
- Strength kcal = `kcalFromMET(strengthMET, weight, strengthMinutes)`
- Activity/cardio kcal = sum of `kcalFromMET(activity.metValue, weight, activity.durationMinutes)` for each activity
- `totalKcal = strengthKcal + activityKcal` (rounded)

#### Duration estimation from sets (`estimateDurationFromSets`)
When `durationMinutes` is absent and sets are available:
```
avgRestSeconds = mean of provided restSeconds values,
                 or 90s default if none provided
totalSeconds   = setCount × (35s per set + avgRestSeconds)
estimatedMinutes = ceil(totalSeconds / 60)
```
Default timing constants:
- `avgSetTimeSeconds = 35`
- `defaultRestSeconds = 90`

#### RPE adjustment for cardio (`getRpeKcalAdjustmentFactor`)
Applied **only to cardio** activities when the user logs an RPE value:
```
factor = 0.9 + (clamp(rpe, 1, 10) / 10) × 0.2
  RPE 1  → ×0.92
  RPE 5  → ×1.00
  RPE 10 → ×1.10
finalKcal = baseKcal × factor
```
**Not applied to lifting** — lifting uses `estimateLiftingCalories()` which has its own RPE model.  
**Not applied to leisure/recovery activities** — these are excluded by name:

```
Excluded keywords (if activity name contains any of these, no RPE adjustment):
"leisure", "easy", "recovery", "warmup", "warm-up", "warm up",
"cooldown", "cool-down", "cool down", "mobility", "stretch",
"stretching", "gentle", "casual", "walking", "walk"
```

`shouldApplyRpeKcalAdjustment(activityName, activityType)` returns `false` for `activityType === "lifting"` or any name matching the exclusion list.

#### Lifting calorie estimation (`estimateLiftingCalories`)
Separate model used for `activityType === "lifting"` entries in `session_activities`:
```typescript
estimateLiftingCalories({
  bodyRegion: 'upper' | 'lower' | 'full',
  durationMinutes: number,
  rpe: number,       // 1–10
  bodyWeightKg: number
}): number
```
METs by body region:
```
lower → 5.5
full  → 5.0
upper → 4.5
```
RPE is baked into this model directly (not via the cardio RPE factor).

#### kcal-per-rep display (`estimateKcalPerRep`)
```typescript
estimateKcalPerRep(totalKcal: number, totalReps: number): number | null
// Returns null if either input is 0; otherwise rounds to 1 decimal
// Purely a rough reference for the user — not medically accurate
```

### 10.2 Training Load System — complete specification

Source file: `server/lib/training-load.ts`

This system turns raw training data (RPE, duration, body region) into a daily load score, classifies it against a personalised baseline, generates natural-language warnings, and surfaces them both as an inline card on the training page and as a modal dialog.

---

#### 10.2.1 Per-activity load score — `computeSessionLoad()`

Every activity in a session contributes a load score:

```
if rpe is present:
  activityLoad = rpe × durationMinutes

else (no RPE — e.g. machine cardio with auto-kcal):
  activityLoad = estimatedKcal  (used as a proxy)
```

A session's contribution is the **sum** of all its activities' load scores.

**Lifting-specific load (for display on activity card, not used in ACWR):**
```
trainingLoadScore = durationMinutes × sessionRpe × bodyRegionMultiplier

bodyRegionMultiplier:
  upper → 1.0
  lower → 1.25
  full  → 1.1
```

---

#### 10.2.2 Day total — `computeDailyLoad()`

Sums `computeSessionLoad()` across all activities for the day.

```typescript
{
  totalLoad:            number      // sum of all activity load scores
  classification:       DayClassification
  provisional:          boolean     // true if it's still today (partial data) or sessions exist but no activities
  sessionCount:         number
  totalDurationMinutes: number
  totalKcal:            number
}
```

**Day classification thresholds — `classifyDayLoad()`**

| `totalLoad` (RPE × minutes) | Classification |
|---|---|
| < 300 | `"light"` |
| 300–599 | `"moderate"` |
| 600–899 | `"hard"` |
| ≥ 900 | `"very_hard"` |

---

#### 10.2.3 ACWR + warning engine — `computeLoadWarnings()`

Takes today's `DailyLoadResult` and an array of prior days (newest-first).

**Step 1 — Acute load (last 7 days)**
```
acuteLoad  = Σ totalLoad for [today, yesterday, …, 6 days ago]
acuteDaily = Math.round((acuteLoad / 7) × 10) / 10
```

**Step 2 — Active day count**
```
activeDaysInWindow = count of days where totalLoad > 0 across all days in the window
insufficientHistory = activeDaysInWindow < 7
```
When `insufficientHistory` is `true`, ACWR and `relativeLoad` are **both forced to `null`** — a baseline built mostly from zero-load rest days would produce spurious high ratios for new users.

**Step 3 — Baseline (28 → 14 → 7 fallback chain)**
```
for n in [28, 14, 7]:
  if totalDaysAvailable >= n:
    baselineLoad    = Math.round((Σ totalLoad[0..n] / n) × 10) / 10
    baselineDaysUsed = n
    break
```

**Step 4 — ACWR**
```
if !insufficientHistory AND baselineLoad > 0:
  acwr = Math.round((acuteDaily / baselineLoad) × 100) / 100
else:
  acwr = null
```

**Step 5 — Relative load (today vs baseline)**
```
if !insufficientHistory AND baselineLoad > 0:
  relativeLoad = Math.round((todayLoad / baselineLoad) × 100) / 100
else:
  relativeLoad = null
```

**Step 6 — Stress flags**

Per-day high-stress determination (`isHighStress()`):
```
if relativeLoad is not null:  high = relativeLoad > 1.2
else (no baseline):           high = totalLoad >= 600
```

Very-high stress:
```
if relativeLoad is not null:  veryHigh = relativeLoad > 1.4
else:                         veryHigh = totalLoad >= 900
```

Stacking flags (uses today, yesterday, and 2-days-ago):
```
backToBackHardDays = todayHigh AND y1High
highLoadCluster    = 2+ of [today, y1, y2] are high-stress
threeDayStreak     = todayHigh AND y1High AND y2High
```

**Step 7 — loadStatus**
```
if acwr === null:  loadStatus = null
elif acwr < 0.8:  loadStatus = "low"
elif acwr <= 1.5: loadStatus = "stable"
else:             loadStatus = "spike"
```

**Step 8 — Warning text generation**

Up to 2 warnings are generated. Priority order: spike/elevated first, stacking second.

```
Condition                        Warning text
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
acwr > 1.5                       "Today's load is well above your recent baseline.
                                  Consider keeping the next session lighter or
                                  prioritising recovery."

relativeLoad > 1.3               "Today's load is above your recent baseline.
(and acwr ≤ 1.5 or acwr null)    A lighter follow-up session or extra recovery
                                  may help."

threeDayStreak = true            "Training stress has been building across the
                                  last 3 days. It may help to reduce intensity
                                  or include a lighter day."

highLoadCluster = true           "Training stress is accumulating across recent
(and not threeDayStreak)         days. Recovery needs may be higher than usual
                                  over the next 24–48 hours."
```

Final list is capped at `warnings.slice(0, 2)`.

---

#### 10.2.4 ACWR risk bands (displayed in `/load-trend`)

| ACWR value | Label | UI colour |
|---|---|---|
| `null` | "No baseline yet" | `text-muted-foreground` |
| < 0.8 | "Under-trained (< 0.8)" | `text-blue-400` |
| 0.8–1.3 | "Optimal zone (0.8–1.3)" | `text-green-400` |
| 1.3–1.5 | "Elevated risk (1.3–1.5)" | `text-yellow-400` |
| > 1.5 | "High risk spike (> 1.5)" | `text-red-400` |

---

#### 10.2.5 `LoadWarningResult` — full returned shape

```typescript
{
  warnings:            string[]         // 0–2 natural-language warning strings
  backToBackHardDays:  boolean
  highLoadCluster:     boolean
  threeDayStreak:      boolean
  acuteLoad:           number           // 7-day sum
  acuteDaily:          number           // acuteLoad / 7 (1dp)
  baselineLoad:        number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:    number | null    // 28, 14, or 7
  acwr:                number | null
  relativeLoad:        number | null    // today / baseline
  highStress:          boolean
  veryHighStress:      boolean
  chronicLoad:         number           // legacy alias for baselineLoad (0 when null)
  loadRatio:           number | null    // alias for acwr
  loadStatus:          "low"|"stable"|"spike"|null
  activeDaysInWindow:  number
  insufficientHistory: boolean
}
```

---

#### 10.2.6 `GET /api/me/training-load/:date` — full response shape

Auth required. Fetches 28 days of history, applies any user override, then runs `computeLoadWarnings()`.

**Override logic:**
- If the user has saved an override for today (`light` or `moderate`), stress flags (`highStress`, `veryHighStress`) are forced false and stress-related warnings are stripped.
- Overrides for prior days are also respected — `light`/`moderate` prior-day overrides feed corrected classifications back into stacking detection.

```typescript
{
  // From DailyLoadResult (today):
  totalLoad:             number
  classification:        "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"
  provisional:           boolean
  sessionCount:          number
  totalDurationMinutes:  number
  totalKcal:             number

  // Added by the route:
  date:                  string   // "YYYY-MM-DD"
  overrideClassification: string | null
  effectiveClassification: "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"  // override ?? classification

  // From LoadWarningResult (spread in):
  warnings:              string[]
  backToBackHardDays:    boolean
  highLoadCluster:       boolean
  threeDayStreak:        boolean
  acuteLoad:             number
  acuteDaily:            number
  baselineLoad:          number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:      number | null
  acwr:                  number | null
  relativeLoad:          number | null
  highStress:            boolean
  veryHighStress:        boolean
  loadStatus:            "low"|"stable"|"spike"|null
  activeDaysInWindow:    number
  insufficientHistory:   boolean
}
```

---

#### 10.2.7 `GET /api/me/training/load-history/:date` — 28-day chart data

Auth required. Returns history in **chronological order** (oldest first) for chart rendering.

```typescript
{
  history: Array<{
    date:           string   // "YYYY-MM-DD"
    totalLoad:      number
    classification: "light"|"moderate"|"hard"|"very_hard"
    relativeLoad:   number | null   // day totalLoad / baselineLoad (null before 7 active days)
    sessionCount:   number
  }>,
  baselineLoad:      number | null
  baselineDaysUsed:  number | null
  acuteLoad:         number
  acuteDaily:        number
  acwr:              number | null
  date:              string   // the reference date used
}
```

---

#### 10.2.8 `POST /api/me/training/load-override/:date` — save user classification

Auth required. Validated values: `"light"` | `"moderate"` | `"hard"` | `"very_hard"`.

```
Request:  { classification: string }
Response: { success: true, overrideClassification: string }
Error:    400 { message: "Invalid classification" }
```

The override is upserted in `training_load_overrides` table. On the next call to `GET /api/me/training-load/:date`, the `effectiveClassification` reflects it and stress warnings are conditionally suppressed.

---

#### 10.2.9 Frontend — inline load insight on the Training page

The training page (`client/src/pages/training.tsx`) fetches load data on every date change:

```typescript
useQuery({
  queryKey: ["/api/me/training-load", selectedDate],
  queryFn: () => fetch(`/api/me/training-load/${selectedDate}`),
  staleTime: 0,   // always re-fetch on mount
})
```

**`dayLoad` useMemo derivation** — determines the badge shown on the training date card:

1. If `trainingLoadData.effectiveClassification` is present → use it (respects overrides)
2. Otherwise fallback: compute locally from `sessions.activities` using the same thresholds

Badge colour mapping:
```
light       bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30
moderate    bg-yellow-500/15 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-500/30
hard        bg-orange-500/15 text-orange-400 border-orange-500/30
very_hard   bg-red-500/15 text-red-400 border-red-500/30
```

If the classification was user-overridden, an `(overridden)` note appears next to the badge.

**Inline warning banners:** When `trainingLoadData.warnings` has entries, each is shown below the classification badge as a small `text-orange-400/70` line with an `AlertTriangle` icon (`data-testid="text-load-warning-{i}"`).

**"28-day trend" link:** Always visible below the warnings. Navigates to `/load-trend`. `data-testid="button-view-load-trend"`.

---

#### 10.2.10 Frontend — `checkAndShowLoadWarning()`

Called automatically after every successful mutation that changes training data:
- After adding a lifting set (`addSetMutation.onSuccess`)
- After adding a cardio/activity (`addActivityMutation.onSuccess`)
- After editing an activity (`editActivityMutation.onSuccess`)

```typescript
async function checkAndShowLoadWarning(date: string) {
  const data = await fetch(`/api/me/training-load/${date}`)
  if (data.warnings.length > 0) {
    _pendingLoadWarning = { analysis: data, date }
    setLoadWarningModal({ open: true, analysis: data })
  }
}
```

**`_pendingLoadWarning` — module-level persistence:**  
Declared at module scope (outside the component), not in React state. This means it survives component unmounts (e.g. navigating away to the trend page and back). On component mount, the `useState` initialiser checks `_pendingLoadWarning` for today's date and re-opens the modal if it hasn't been acknowledged yet.

---

#### 10.2.11 Frontend — `TrainingLoadWarningModal`

Component: `client/src/components/TrainingLoadWarningModal.tsx`  
`data-testid="modal-load-warning"`

**Trigger:** Shown when `loadWarningModal.open === true` (set by `checkAndShowLoadWarning`).

**Cannot be dismissed** by clicking outside or pressing Escape — `onInteractOutside` and `onEscapeKeyDown` both call `e.preventDefault()`. The only way to close it is the "Continue" button.

**Layout — three sections:**

1. **Metrics row** (3 equal columns):
   - Today — `analysis.totalLoad` / "load pts"
   - Baseline — `Math.round(analysis.baselineLoad)` / `{N}d avg` (or `"< 7 days"` if null)
   - ACWR — `analysis.acwr.toFixed(2)` / "ratio" (or `"building baseline"` when `insufficientHistory`)

2. **Sparse history notice** (shown only when `analysis.insufficientHistory === true`):
   > "We're still building your training baseline. Until you have at least 7 training days logged, load insights use simple thresholds."

3. **System estimate badge** — `effectiveClassification` displayed with colour coding:
   ```
   light       bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30
   moderate    bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-500/30
   hard        bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400 border-orange-500/30
   very_hard   bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border-red-500/30
   ```

4. **Warning list** — each warning in a `bg-yellow-500/5 border-yellow-500/20` container. Icon logic:
   - Warning text contains "spike" → `TrendingUp` in `text-red-400`
   - Warning text contains "elevated" → `TrendingUp` in `text-orange-400`
   - Otherwise → `AlertTriangle` in `text-yellow-400`
   - `data-testid="load-warning-{i}"`

5. **Override select** (`data-testid="select-load-override"`):
   ```
   Options:  "Use system estimate" (value="keep") | "Light day" | "Moderate day" | "Hard day" | "Very hard day"
   ```
   When a non-`keep` value is selected, a hint appears: *"Your rating will be saved for this day and used to reduce unnecessary warnings."*

6. **No-baseline notice** (when `analysis.baselineLoad === null`):
   > "You have fewer than 7 days of data. Thresholds are based on absolute load until your baseline is established."

**Actions:**

- **"Continue"** (`data-testid="button-load-acknowledge"`) — if an override was chosen, calls `POST /api/me/training/load-override/{date}` first, then clears `_pendingLoadWarning` and closes the modal.
- **"View 28-day load trend"** (`data-testid="button-view-load-trend"`) — navigates to `/load-trend` **without** closing or acknowledging the modal. The modal re-opens when the user navigates back because `_pendingLoadWarning` is still set.

---

#### 10.2.12 Frontend — Load Trend page (`/load-trend`)

Route: `client/src/pages/load-trend.tsx`  
Data: `GET /api/me/training/load-history/{today}`

**4 summary stat cards:**

| Card label | Value | Sub-label |
|---|---|---|
| ACWR | `data.acwr.toFixed(2)` or `"—"` | ACWR status label (see §10.2.4) |
| Baseline | `Math.round(data.baselineLoad)` or `"—"` | `"{N}-day avg"` or `"< 7 days data"` |
| Acute (7d) | `data.acuteLoad` | `"{data.acuteDaily.toFixed(0)}/day avg"` |
| High-stress | count of days where `relativeLoad > 1.2` (or `totalLoad >= 600` if no baseline) | `"of {trainingDays} training days"` |

**Chart 1 — Absolute Load** (always shown):
- Type: `ComposedChart` with a single `Bar` series (`dataKey="totalLoad"`)
- X-axis: `date`, formatted `"d MMM"`, tick interval 6
- Y-axis: raw load units
- Reference lines (dashed):
  - `y=300` — green `#22c55e` (light/moderate boundary)
  - `y=600` — orange `#f97316` (moderate/hard boundary)
  - `y=900` — red `#ef4444` (hard/very_hard boundary)
  - `y=baselineLoad` — primary colour, labelled `"baseline"` (only when baselineLoad is set)
- Bar fill: `hsl(var(--primary))` at `opacity=0.75`, corner radius `[2,2,0,0]`

**Chart 2 — Relative Load** (only shown when at least one entry has `relativeLoad !== null`):
- Type: `ComposedChart` with a single `Bar` series (`dataKey="relativeLoad"`)
- Y-axis: formatted with `×` suffix
- Reference lines:
  - `y=1.0` — muted, dashed (baseline = 1)
  - `y=1.2` — yellow `#eab308`, labelled `"high stress"`
  - `y=1.4` — red `#ef4444`, labelled `"very high"`
- Sub-note: *"1.0 = exactly at baseline · >1.2 high stress · >1.4 very high stress"*

**Custom tooltip** — shown on bar hover:
```
Date (formatted "EEE d MMM")
Load      {totalLoad}
Relative  {relativeLoad.toFixed(2)}×   (if not null)
Class     {classification}             (coloured)
Sessions  {sessionCount}               (if > 0)
```

**ACWR education card** (always at the bottom):
> "The Acute:Chronic Workload Ratio (ACWR) compares your 7-day average load to your baseline. Research suggests the 'sweet spot' is **0.8–1.3** — below this suggests detraining, above 1.5 indicates injury risk elevation."
> "Baseline window: 28 days → 14 days → 7 days as your history builds."
> Citation: *Gabbett, T.J. (2016). British Journal of Sports Medicine, 50(5), 273–280.*

---

#### 10.2.13 Classification colour reference (all UI contexts)

| Classification | Badge text | Bar colour | Badge CSS classes |
|---|---|---|---|
| `light` | Light | `#22c55e` | `bg-green-500/20 text-green-400` |
| `moderate` | Moderate | `#eab308` | `bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400` |
| `hard` | Hard | `#f97316` | `bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400` |
| `very_hard` | Very Hard | `#ef4444` | `bg-red-500/20 text-red-400` |

Note: the training page day-badge uses slightly different opacity variants (`/15` background, `/30` border) while the modal uses `/20` background, `/30` border.

### 10.3 `computeLoadWarnings()` — see §10.2.3 above

## 11. Food Logging System

### 11.1 Entry sources
1. **Manual** — user types macros directly
2. **Core Foods Quick-Add** — pre-curated list of common meals (see §12)
3. **Open Food Facts search** — barcode or text search via `/api/foods/search`
4. **Barcode scan** — html5-qrcode → `/api/food/barcode/:code`
5. **Saved Meals (templates)** — one-tap log of a saved meal template
6. **Copy from another day** — `/api/me/meals/copy`
7. **AI Quick Log** — natural language → `AILogDialog.tsx`

### 11.2 Raw vs cooked weight
Each entry has `enteredBasis: 'raw'|'cooked'` and `isRawWeight: boolean`.  
The server applies a **cook-factor conversion** to standardise all entries to cooked weight before calculating macros/micros.  
Typical factors (stored in `ingredients.json`): rice raw→cooked ≈ 0.4, chicken raw→cooked ≈ 0.75.

### 11.3 Micronutrient resolution chain

`getFoodMicrosForDate()` in `server/lib/micros.ts` processes each food entry in this priority order:

**Step 1 — Composite food name match (highest priority)**  
Check `entry.name.toLowerCase().trim()` against the `COMPOSITE_FOODS` map (see §13).  
If matched:
- Scale each component's gram weight by `loggedGrams / referenceServing`
- Look up each component in `ingredients.json` by case-insensitive name
- Sum `(micro_per_100g × componentGrams) / 100` for each of the 17 `MICRO_KEYS`
- This path is followed for **all** core food quick-add entries

**Step 2 — OFF entry with ingredient mapping**  
If `entry.sourceType === "off"` AND `entry.microSource === "ingredient"` AND `entry.ingredientIndex` is a valid number:
- Look up `ingredients[ingredientIndex]` directly (by array position, not name)
- Sum `(micro_per_100g × entryGrams) / 100`
- This path is followed when the user has mapped a scanned barcode to an ingredient

**Step 3 — Manual entry name fallback**  
If `entry.sourceType !== "off"`:
- Case-insensitive name search in `ingredients.json` (`i.name.toLowerCase() === entry.name.toLowerCase()`)
- If matched, use that ingredient's micros
- Allows whole-food manual entries (e.g. "Chicken breast") to get micros automatically

**Step 4 — No micros**  
OFF entries without a valid mapping (`microSource !== "ingredient"`) are skipped entirely — they contribute zero to AMQS.

#### Micro key lookup helper (`getMicronutrientValue`)
```typescript
// From shared/utils.ts
getMicronutrientValue(ingredient, `${key}_per_100g`)
// Returns null if the key doesn't exist on the ingredient object
```

#### How core foods map to scanned/OFF foods
Core food quick-adds work via **name-based composite matching** (Step 1 above) — no `ingredientIndex` is needed.  
When a user scans a barcode for a product that is similar to a core food (e.g., a branded porridge), the barcode flow runs separately and the user can map it to an ingredient via `/api/food/barcode/:code/map`. The mapping writes `ingredientIndex` and `microSource: "ingredient"` to the `food_entries` row, enabling Step 2 on future lookups.

### 11.4 Barcode flow
1. Client sends barcode to `/api/food/barcode/:code`
2. Server checks `off_product_mappings` for existing mapping
3. If not found → fetches from Open Food Facts API
4. If found with high-confidence match → returns ingredient micros automatically
5. If low confidence → client shows "map to ingredient" UI for the user to pick
6. User selection saved via `/api/food/barcode/:code/map`

### 11.5 Meal sections
Meals: `breakfast`, `lunch`, `dinner`, `snack`  
Snacks are numbered with `snackIndex` (0, 1, 2…) to support multiple snack slots.

### 11.6 Macro warnings
Visual warnings appear when logged macros exceed targets by >10%.

---

## 11.7 Quick Log — AI-Assisted Natural Language Logging

Quick Log lets the user describe what they've done in plain English. The parser classifies the text client-side, shows a confirmation screen, and only writes to the database after the user taps a confirm button. **Nothing is saved during parsing.**

---

### 11.7.1 Entry point — dashboard header button

**Location:** Dashboard header action bar, alongside "Add Food", "Log Weight", and "Log Macros".

```tsx
<Button
  variant="outline"
  size="default"
  onClick={() => setAiLogOpen(true)}
  data-testid="button-ai-log"
>
  <Sparkles className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
  Quick Log
</Button>
```

`AILogDialog` is mounted once at the top of the dashboard `return()`:

```tsx
<AILogDialog
  open={aiLogOpen}
  onOpenChange={setAiLogOpen}
  date={selectedDate}
  onSuccess={() => setAiLogOpen(false)}
/>
```

---

### 11.7.2 Dialog structure — 4 states

**File:** `client/src/components/AILogDialog.tsx`

```
DialogState = "input" | "review" | "saving" | "done"
```

| State | What the user sees |
|---|---|
| `input` | Textarea + optional mic icon + "Review" button |
| `review` | Intent-specific confirmation card with editable fields |
| `saving` | Confirm button shows spinner (mutation pending) |
| `done` | Success screen with "Log another" button |

**Dialog container:** `sm:max-w-md`  
**Title:** Sparkles icon + `"Quick Log"` (font-display)

---

### 11.7.3 Input state UI

```
DialogHeader: Sparkles icon + "Quick Log"

Description (text-xs text-muted-foreground):
  "Describe what you want to log in plain language.
   You'll review everything before it's saved."

Textarea (relative wrapper):
  value={inputText}
  placeholder: "e.g. '2 eggs and toast for breakfast' ·
                'Morning weight 71.8' · 'Pads 60 min at 7pm'"
  className="pr-10 resize-none min-h-[80px]"
  data-testid="ai-log-input"
  onKeyDown: Cmd/Ctrl+Enter → handleParse()
  
  [Mic button] (absolute right-2 top-2, only if SpeechRecognition supported):
    idle:      Mic icon, text-muted-foreground
    listening: MicOff icon, text-red-400 bg-red-500/10
    data-testid="ai-mic-button"

[If isListening]:
  "● Listening — speak naturally, stops after 3s silence"  (text-red-400)
  interim text shown as italic muted text

Button row:
  [Review] flex-1, disabled when inputText.trim() empty
    <Edit2 /> Review
    data-testid="ai-parse-button"
  [Cancel] variant=ghost → onOpenChange(false)

Footer (text-[10px] text-muted-foreground text-center opacity-60):
  "Cmd/Ctrl+Enter to review · Nothing is saved until you confirm"
```

---

### 11.7.4 Parser — `client/src/lib/aiLogParser.ts`

💻 **CLIENT-SIDE ONLY.** No network requests made during parsing.

#### Pipeline

```
1. Normalise input (lowercase, trim)
2. Score all 5 intents using keyword banks + regex
3. Pick highest-scoring intent (minimum score: 2)
4. Sub-parse to extract structured entities
5. Return typed ParseResult with requiresConfirmation: true
```

#### Intent priority order (scored simultaneously, highest wins)

| Intent | Trigger condition |
|---|---|
| `create_recurring_training_schedule` | `"every [weekday]"` pattern |
| `log_weight` | Weight trigger phrase (`"weight"`, `"weigh"`, `"bw"`) + numeric extraction |
| `log_training_session` | Activity keyword match (from `TRAINING_ACTIVITY_KEYWORDS`) |
| `log_supplements` | Supplement keyword match + optionally a "taken/took" verb |
| `log_food` | Meal keyword / food trigger phrase + extractable food items |
| `unknown` | No intent scores ≥ 2 |

#### Scoring functions

| Intent | Key signals | Score examples |
|---|---|---|
| recurring | `every [day]` pattern | +4; matching training keyword +1 |
| weight | weight trigger phrase | +3; extracted numeric weight +4 |
| training | activity keyword | +3; duration present +2; time of day +1 |
| supplements | per keyword match | +2 each; taken/took verb +2 |
| food | food trigger phrase | +2; meal keyword +2; each food item +2 (max +6) |

#### Intent types and ParseResult shapes

```typescript
// All intents share these base fields:
// requiresConfirmation: true (always)
// rawInput: string
// confidence: "high" | "medium" | "low"
// missingFields: string[]

ParsedFood: {
  intent: "log_food";
  meal: "breakfast" | "lunch" | "dinner" | "snack";
  items: FoodItem[];  // { rawText, normalizedName, count?, sizeHint?, gramsHint? }
}

ParsedWeight: {
  intent: "log_weight";
  weightKg: number;  // auto-converts lbs → kg
}

ParsedTraining: {
  intent: "log_training_session";
  activityName: string;   // canonical catalog name (from ACTIVITY_CANONICAL_NAME map)
  durationMinutes: number; // defaults 60 if not detected
  timeOfDay: "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening";
  timeLabel?: string;       // e.g. "7pm"
}

ParsedSupplements: {
  intent: "log_supplements";
  items: string[];   // matched supplement display names (title-cased)
}

ParsedRecurring: {
  intent: "create_recurring_training_schedule";
  dayOfWeek: string;   // full day name e.g. "Tuesday"
  scope?: "fight camp" | "general";
  sessions: RecurringSession[];
}

ParsedUnknown: {
  intent: "unknown";
  clarificationHint: string;
}
```

#### Confidence levels

| Level | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `high` | Multiple strong signals (meal keyword + food items, or weight trigger + number) |
| `medium` | Single strong signal or ambiguous detection |
| `low` | Parser uncertain |

Displayed as a coloured `<Badge>` in the review card:
- `high` → emerald (`bg-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-400`)
- `medium` → yellow
- `low` → red

#### Ingredient matching (food intent only)

After parsing, `AILogDialog` fuzzy-matches each `FoodItem.normalizedName` against `GET /api/ingredients` (loaded once, `staleTime: 5min`). The matching algorithm (`matchIngredient`):

1. Exact name match → score 100
2. Name starts with query → 80
3. Name contains query → 60
4. Query contains name → 50
5. Word-by-word overlap (≥3 chars) → 15 per overlapping word

Macros calculated: `Math.round(nutrient_per_100g × grams / 100)`

Gram resolution order:
1. Explicit `gramsHint` from parser (e.g. "100g of chicken")
2. `count × coreFoodUnit` grams (from `coreFoodUnits.ts`)
3. `count × 100`
4. Default: 100g

#### Activity canonicalisation

The parser maps raw activity keywords to catalog-search terms before hitting `/api/activities`:

```
"pads"   → "Muay Thai"
"bjj"    → "Judo/Jiu-Jitsu"
"lifting"→ "Strength Training"
"run"    → "Running (moderate)"
// etc. (full map in ACTIVITY_CANONICAL_NAME in aiLogParser.ts)
```

---

### 11.7.5 Review state — 6 intent-specific cards

#### 1. Food review card (`log_food`)

```
Meal badge (capitalize) + ConfidenceBadge
"Log this meal?"

Per-item rows (space-y-2):
  div className="flex items-start gap-3 rounded-lg border p-3 text-sm"
    [toggle button] data-testid="ai-food-toggle-{i}"
      confirmed → CheckCircle2 (text-emerald-400)
      rejected  → XCircle (text-muted-foreground)
    [item details]:
      if matched → ingredient name + inline grams input + macros
        grams input: className="w-14 bg-secondary/50 rounded px-1 py-0.5 text-xs text-center font-mono"
                     data-testid="ai-food-grams-{i}"
                     onChange → recalculates macros live
        macro display: "{grams}g  {kcal} kcal  {P}g P  {C}g C  {F}g F"
      if unmatched → italic muted "Unrecognised: "{name}" — deselected"
  
  [if unmatched items exist]:
    "{n} item(s) not matched to the ingredient list — they will be skipped.
     Use "Add Food" to log them manually."

  [if confirmed items > 0]:
    totals bar: "Total: {kcal} kcal  {P}g protein"  (bg-secondary/40)

  [Log {n} item(s)] data-testid="ai-confirm-food"   disabled: confirmed=0 || saving
  [← Edit]          data-testid="ai-edit-back"       → setDialogState("input")
```

On confirm: `POST /api/food` for each confirmed+matched item with:
```json
{
  "date": "...",
  "name": "{ingredient.name}",
  "grams": {grams},
  "calories": {n}, "protein": {n}, "carbs": {n}, "fat": {n}, "fibre": {n},
  "meal": "{meal}",
  "sourceType": "ingredient",
  "ingredientIndex": {n},
  "macroSource": "ingredient",
  "microSource": "ingredient"
}
```
Cache invalidated: `["/api/me/food/{date}"]`, `["/api/me/amqs/score"]`

#### 2. Weight review card (`log_weight`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Log morning weight?"

Row (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3):
  Large mono weight display  +  editable input
  input step=0.1 min=30 max=250  data-testid="ai-weight-input"
  
"Date: {EEE d MMM yyyy}"

[Confirm] data-testid="ai-confirm-weight"   disabled: !weightValue || saving
[← Edit]  data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

On confirm: `POST /api/weights` with `{ date, weight: weightValue }`  
Cache invalidated: `weights/range`, `weight-cut`, `targets/effective`, `morning-status`

#### 3. Training review card (`log_training_session`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Log this training session?"

Card (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3 space-y-3):
  Activity:  inline text input  data-testid="ai-training-activity"
             onChange → also updates activitySearchQ for catalog suggestions
  
  [Activity suggestions] (if activitySearchQ ≥ 2 chars):
    Fetches GET /api/activities?query={q}   staleTime 60s
    Shows up to 5 pill-buttons  data-testid="activity-suggestion-{id}"
    Click → sets activityName, clears search
  
  Duration:  number input (min=1)  data-testid="ai-training-duration"  + "min"
  Time:      <select> morning/afternoon/evening  data-testid="ai-training-timeoday"
  Date:      read-only "{EEE d MMM}"

[If duration not detected]: yellow warning "Duration was not detected — defaulted to 60 min."

[Log Session] data-testid="ai-confirm-training"   disabled: !activityName || saving
[← Edit]      data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

On confirm, 3 sequential API calls:
1. `POST /api/workouts/sessions` → `{ date, timeOfDay, title: activityName, intensity: "moderate" }`
2. `GET /api/activities?query={activityName}` → find best-match MET value
3. `POST /api/workouts/sessions/{id}/activities` → `{ name, durationMinutes, intensity: "moderate", activityType: "cardio", metValue: bestActivity.metValue ?? 6, activityCatalogId }`

Cache invalidated: `workouts/sessions`, `training/summary`, `targets/effective`

#### 4. Supplements review card (`log_supplements`)

```
ConfidenceBadge
"Mark as taken?"

Per-supplement rows:
  [toggle] data-testid="ai-supp-toggle-{i}"
  Raw name (user input)
  if matched:   "→ {supplement.name}" (text-muted-foreground)
  if unmatched: "Not found in your supplements — will be skipped" (text-yellow-400)

[If no matches]:
  "None of the named supplements matched your saved list.
   Add them in the Supplements section first, then log them here."

[Mark Taken] data-testid="ai-confirm-supplements"  disabled: !hasMatches || saving
[← Edit]     data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

Supplement matching uses `GET /api/me/supplements` (loaded when dialog opens). The `matchSupplement` function uses the same fuzzy scoring as ingredient matching.

On confirm: `POST /api/supplement-intakes` for each matched+included item:
```json
{ "supplementId": {id}, "stackId": {id | null}, "date": "...", "taken": true }
```
Cache invalidated: `["/api/me/supplement-intakes/{date}"]`

#### 5. Recurring training card (`create_recurring_training_schedule`)

```
ConfidenceBadge  +  optional "Fight Camp" badge (if scope = "fight camp")
"Create {dayOfWeek} sessions?"

Notice (text-xs text-muted-foreground):
  "V1: This will create sessions for the next {dayOfWeek} ({formatted date}) only.
   Full recurring scheduling can be set up in the Training Log."

Per-session cards (rounded-lg border bg-card p-3):
  Activity name
  timeLabel (if present) · timeOfDay · {durationMinutes} min

[Create Next {dayOfWeek}] data-testid="ai-confirm-recurring"  disabled: saving
[← Edit]                  data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

Date target: `getNextDayDate(dayOfWeek)` — finds the next occurrence of that weekday (always ≥ 1 day ahead).

On confirm: for each session, same 3-step sequence as single training (POST session → lookup activity → POST activity).

#### 6. Unknown intent card

```
Yellow warning box:
  "Not sure what to log"
  {clarificationHint}

Suggestion list:
  "2 eggs and 2 slices of toast for breakfast"
  "Morning weight 71.8"
  "Pads for 60 min at 7pm"
  "Creatine and Vitamin D taken"

[← Try again] data-testid="ai-edit-back"
```

### 11.7.6 Done state

```
CheckCircle2 (h-12 w-12 text-emerald-400)
"Logged successfully"

[Log another] variant=outline  data-testid="ai-log-another"
  → resets dialogState, inputText, parsed  + calls onSuccess()
```

---

### 11.7.7 Voice input (Web Speech API)

Microphone button only renders when `window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition` is truthy.

```
recognition.lang = "en-GB"
recognition.continuous = true
recognition.interimResults = true
recognition.maxAlternatives = 1
```

Silence timer: 3 000 ms (`SILENCE_TIMEOUT_MS`). Resets on every `onresult` event. When it fires, `stopListening()` is called.

Final transcript chunks are **appended** to `inputText` (space-separated). Interim transcript is shown below the textarea as italic text while the user speaks.

---

### 11.7.8 Data loaded on dialog open

| Data | Query key | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| Ingredient list | `["/api/ingredients"]` | Food item → macro lookup. `staleTime: 5min`. |
| User supplements | `["/api/me/supplements"]` | Supplement name matching |
| Activity suggestions | `["/api/activities", searchQ]` | Training review catalog typeahead. Only runs when `searchQ.length ≥ 2`. `staleTime: 60s`. |

---

| Supplement include/exclude toggle | `ai-supp-toggle-{index}` |
| Recurring confirm | `ai-confirm-recurring` |
| Back / Edit button (all review cards) | `ai-edit-back` |
| Log another button (done state) | `ai-log-another` |

---

### 11.7.10 Extending the parser

| Task | File | What to edit |
|---|---|---|
| Add a new activity keyword | `client/src/lib/aiLogParser.ts` | `TRAINING_ACTIVITY_KEYWORDS` array |
| Map a keyword to a catalog name | `client/src/lib/aiLogParser.ts` | `ACTIVITY_CANONICAL_NAME` record |
| Add a supplement keyword | `client/src/lib/aiLogParser.ts` | `SUPPLEMENT_KEYWORDS` array |
| Add core food unit support (count → grams) | `client/src/lib/coreFoodUnits.ts` | Follow `docs/core_food_units.md` |
